Forward 
Overview 
VMS is a digital and intelligent video management platform comprised of seven core 
modules: Monitoring Center, Event Center, Intelligent Search, Access Control, Parking 
Management, Intelligent Analysis, and Operation and Maintenance Center, along 
with two subsystems for Retail and Energy. The system employs a Client/Server (C/S) 
architecture based on a Service-Oriented Architecture (SOA), allowing for clear 
functionality of service modules and maintaining loose coupling between services, 
which facilitates module reuse and flexible expansion. The system supports All-In-
One deployment for all services and also allows for distributed deployment to 
achieve elastic scaling for medium to large project scenarios. Additionally, VMS is a 
fully open northbound system that defines a comprehensive set of open APIs. These 
open northbound APIs enable rapid integration between third-party applications and 
the VMS platform. 
Target Audience 
This document is mainly for developers of third-party manufacturers who want to 
develop applications based on DSS open capabilities. 
To better understand the content of this document, the following technical skills are 
required: 
 Proficiency in programming languages such as Java and C#. 
 Familiarity with the security industry, including understanding terms related to 
video surveillance, alarms, and PTZ (Pan-Tilt-Zoom) cameras. 
 A good understanding of video-related protocols, including knowledge of the 
usage of RTSP (Real Time Streaming Protocol) and HTTP (Hypertext Transfer 
Protocol). 
Dahua-HTTP-API-For-DSS-V8.7_EN for pt_era_baru_digitama

Terms 
Terms/ 
Abbreviation 
Description 
VMS Video Management Platform 
TLS Transport Layer Security  
HTTPS 
The HTTP channel aimed at security ensures the integrity of the 
transmission process through encryption and authentication based on 
HTTP. 
RTSP 
Real-time streaming protocol is specially used to control the transmission 
of multimedia streams, which can play, pause and stop the video stream 
through a series of commands. 
RTP Real-time Transport Protocol 
FLV Flash Video 
HLS HTTP Live Streaming 
Token After a user successfully logs in to the VMS platform, the platform will 
automatically assign a token as the unique credential of the user 
Organization The platform defaults to a root organization, which can encompass sub-
organizations as well as devices. 
Device Referring to a physical device, such as an NVR, IPC, access control or alarm 
hub 
Unit 
The platform categorizes devices into multiple units based on their 
capabilities. Unit types include encoding units, decoding units, alarm input 
units, alarm output units, among others. A single device may contain 
multiple units. 
Channel 
Each unit contains multiple channels, with channels being the smallest 
units that provide data capabilities. For example, an encoding channel can 
output video stream data, while an alarm channel can detect and output 
alarms.

1 Overview 
1.1 Instruction 
To quickly understand the API capabilities offered by the VMS platform and expedite 
development, please follow the document content in the order provided below. 
[Forward]: Explain the business capabilities and architecture of the VMS platform, and 
provide a preliminary understanding of the technical terms that will appear in the 
document. 
[Overview]: Describe the open capabilities of the VMS platform and introduce 
integration solutions for different scenarios, providing a preliminary understanding of the 
integration process. 
[Interface Specification]: Introduce the calling specifications for the VMS Open API and 
the MQ message push specifications. 
[API Interface]: Categorize the APIs for easy search, allowing developers to understand 
specific functions and usage methods through API descriptions and usage examples. 
Developers can then select the required API interfaces. 
[MQ Notification Message]: Developers should pay attention to this section when they 
need to receive real-time notifications or alerts from the platform. Notifications can be 
categorized for easy searching, allowing developers to understand specific functions and 
usage methods through descriptions and examples. They can then subscribe to the 
necessary notification messages. 
[Best Practice]: This section provides detailed integration methods for commonly used 
platform features through several classic integration cases, enabling developers to gain a 
deeper understanding of how to use the platform API effectively. 
[Appendix]: The data dictionary, error code and code example DEMO of the platform are 
provided for the developer's reference. There are API login authentication example 
DEMO, MQ docking example DEMO, and encryption and decryption example DEMO. 
[FAQ]: Provide solutions for common issues encountered during the integration process. 
Dahua-HTTP-API-For-DSS-V8.7_EN for pt_era_baru_digitama

1.2 Architecture 
The VMS (Video Management System) platform provides comprehensive management 
capabilities for video, alarms, access control, attendance, personnel, vehicles, parking lots, 
facial recognition, and structured data. It defines standard REST API interfaces for open 
access, allowing third-party developers to interact with the platform via HTTPS. 
Additionally, developers can receive real-time notifications from the platform through 
subscribed MQ messages.  
For video services, the platform supports pulling streams directly via RTSP, FLV, and HLS 
protocols. To address the complexity of video services and facilitate third-party 
integration, it provides a packaged DPSDK.dll for client and app integration, as well as a 
JS package for Web plug-in integration. Third-party developers can choose the 
appropriate integration method based on their specific requirements. 
The architecture is as follows:

1.3 Preparation 
Step 1: Prepare the VMS environment 
 Install the VMS platform 
Get the installation package, install the platform according to the platform user’s 
manual, and then enable all the services. 
Dahua-HTTP-API-For-DSS-V8.7_EN for pt_era_baru_digitama

--- PAGE 10 ---
 
9 
 
 Install the VMS client 
Get the client installation package and install it. Configure the login account. The 
default user is system.  
 Import the License 
Get the valid activation code of the License, and import the License to the 
platform to authenticate the platform. 
 Adding Devices 
Add front-end equipment to the platform to ensure that the platform has 
accessible front-end codec resources. 
 Select the Language 
Select a suitable programming language that facilitates interaction with 
protocols such as HTTP, MQ, and RTSP. If video playback functionality is 
required, incorporate the implementation of the playback component as well. 
The platform offers two access methods: HTTP (unencrypted) and HTTPS 
(encrypted). The default access port for HTTP is port 80, while the default port 
for HTTPS is 443. During the development and debugging phase, HTTP can be 
used for easier packet capturing and troubleshooting. In actual usage, HTTPS 
must be employed to ensure the security of information transmission. To enable 
access via HTTP on port 80, the client must configure the HTTP allowlist in the 
[System Parameters -> Security Configuration] page, adding the IP addresses of 
third-party developer machines to the allowlist. 
Step 2 Select the integration method based on the scenario. 
VMS provides various integration methods for different scenarios. Third-party 
developers can choose the appropriate integration method based on their 
business requirements and development languages. 
 Directly integrating with the video service using DPSDK.dll allows you to 
utilize the DPSDK integration method without needing to focus on the API 
documentation. Please refer to the DPSDK usage instructions for guidance. 
The download link for DPSDK is: 
https://depp.dahuasecurity.com/integration/guide/download/DSS%20SDK. 
Dahua-HTTP-API-For-DSS-V8.7_EN for pt_era_baru_digitama

--- PAGE 11 ---
 
10 
 
 Integrate with the video service using the API along with a Web plugin. 
Please contact DSS marketing personnel to obtain the Web plugin. 
 Integrate with the video service using the API combined with FLV/HLS. The 
default baseline installation package of DSS does not support FLV/HLS 
streaming. Please contact DSS marketing personnel to obtain the installation 
package for FLV/HLS services and install it in the DSS environment. 
 Integrate with the video service using the API with the RTSP method. This is 
supported by the default DSS baseline installation. 
 Non-video services need to be integrated using the API method. 
Step 3 Integrated with VMS 
 After the third-party developers obtain the username and password for 
logging into the VMS and confirm the integration method, they can start 
integrating with the VMS. 
1.4 Integration Process 
The API integration with VMS involves 3 steps: 
Log in and authenticate through the HTTP Digest method-> Obtain MQ configuration 
and subscribe to MQ notification message-> Call the business interface to complete 
business docking. The process is as follows:

2 Interface Specifications 
2.1 HTTP Interface Protocol Specification 
All APIs provided by VMS are based on the HTTP/1.1 protocol and follow RESTful 
principles. Data exchanged is standardized in JSON format. VMS defaults to open HTTPS 
ports and does not recommend using HTTP for calls. To enable HTTP access, the allowlist 
for port 80 must be configured in VMS (System Parameters -> Security Configuration -> 
HTTP Allowlist). 
Item Description 
Transmission 
Method To ensure the security of transmission, uses HTTPS transmission. 
URL format 
http(s)://[platform ip]:[platform 
port]/[subsystem]/api/[version]/[module]/[interface]/... For detail, see the rules 
of URL below. 
Request Method GET / POST / PUT / DELETE 
Data Format All in JSON format for the request and response data. 
Character 
Encoding Using UTF-8 encoding 
Safety 
Authentication 
Access to the API is secured through username/password authentication; only 
users who successfully authenticate and obtain a Token can access the API. 
Permission 
Control 
Most APIs are controlled by VMS menu permissions. Calling an unauthorized 
API will result in an error message. 
Certificate 
Requirements None 
Calling Result See the instruction on HTTP returned parameters. 
2.1.1 Request Instructions 
 Request Methods: 
Request 
Method 
Operation 
POST Obtain resources, mostly used for business data query and data acquisition. 
Dahua-HTTP-API-For-DSS-V8.7_EN for pt_era_baru_digitama

--- PAGE 14 ---
 
13 
 
Request 
Method 
Operation 
GET Resource creation and data submission, primarily used for sending data to the 
backend or inserting it into a database. 
PUT Resource updating, primarily used for refreshing backend caches, databases, 
etc. 
DELETE Resource deletion, primarily used for removing data records. 
 URL Instructions: 
The HTTP request URL format is as follows: http(s)://[platform ip]:[platform 
port]/[subsystem]/api/[version]/[module]/[interface]/... 
Item Instruction 
ip VMS IP address 
port Port Number 
subsystem Sub-system name, including brms, obms, ipms, iams and more 
version 
API versioning is indicated by "V" followed by the major version and 
minor version, such as v1.0 or v1.1. The major version number changes 
when there are breaking changes, while the minor version number 
changes when new features are added. 
module Module name, can be omitted. 
interface Port name 
In the format above, the ellipsis (...) may represent multiple hierarchical nodes in the 
resource description (e.g., node1/node2), depending on the specific context. 
The completed example is as follows: 
# new resources  
POST /brms/api/v1.1/user  
# resource acquisition 
GET /brms/api/v1.1/user/{id}  
# resource update  
PUT /brms/api/v1.1/user/{id} 不 
# resource upate (an attribute)  
PUT /brms/api/v1.1/user/{id}/password  
# resource operation  
PUT /brms/api/v1.1/user/{id}/lock  
# resource deletion  
DELETE /brms/api/v1.1/ user/{id} 
# delete in batches (Parameters are simple and do not exceed the Uri length limit)  
DELETE /brms/api/v1.1/user?ids={ids}  
# delete in batches (Parameter is complex or may exceed Uri length limit)  
POST /brms/api/v1.1/user/delete/batch  
# search for ( list) 
GET /brms/api/v1.1/user/list  
# search for (page)  
GET /brms/api/v1.1/user/page

2.1.2 Response Instructions 
The status code of HTTP interface call success is uniformly 200 (401 will be returned for 
individual interface authentication failure). Various exceptions at the business level are 
uniformly reflected by returning the code field and desc in the body. 
Parameter Type Description 
code int 
Error code: 1000 indicates success, while any code other than 
1000 indicates a failure. Common error codes can be found in 
Appendix 6.2. 
Dahua-HTTP-API-For-DSS-V8.7_EN for pt_era_baru_digitama

--- PAGE 17 ---
 
16 
 
Parameter Type Description 
desc string Description of the code 
data object The result data: the data content for different business 
interfaces is not fixed.

Example 1: (no data)

    "code": 1000,  
"desc": "Success",

2.2 Specification of MQ Message Subscription and Push 
Notifications from the VMS platform are pushed in real-time to clients or third parties via 
ActiveMQ. Therefore, developers must subscribe to the MQ message queue as needed 
according to VMS specifications to receive real-time notifications or alerts from the VMS. 
The protocol body uses JSON format. The message body format is consistent for both the 
sending and receiving queues. 
Request Parameter: 
Parameter Type Description 
id string SN 
method string Method 
info object Message content 
Example of message body: 
{ 
    "id": "112456",  
    "method": "...",  
    "info":  
    { 
        ... 
    } 
} 
Currently, the VMS platform has 4 topics that require subscription: 
The userId and userGroupId represent the ID of the logged-in user and the user group ID, 
respectively. The login authentication interface returns the current user's userId and 
userGroupId. For example, if the current user's userId is 1 and the userGroupId is 2, the 
topics to subscribe to are: 
Parameter Type Example 
Alarm topic 
mq.alarm.msg.topic.{userId} 
mq.alarm.msg.group.topic.{userGroupId} 
mq.alarm.msg.topic.1 
mq.alarm.msg.group.topic.2 
Event topic mq.event.msg.topic.{userId} mq.event.msg.topic.1 
Public topic mq.common.msg.topic mq.common.msg.topic 
The messages pushed by the MQ are in JSON format. The specific format can be 
referenced in the MQ message.

Obtain platform image resources. For security reasons, append the resource access 
credential to the image URL in the following format: Url?token={credential}. This 
credential is solely used for downloading platform files, while uploading files to the 
platform requires a login token. The credential is derived from the response during 
platform login; refer to section [3.1.2 Submit Credentials] for the returned credential. An 
example of a complete download image URL is as follows: 
https://192.168.1.1:9901/56602311-65f5-11eb-94b1-4cedfb428a36/20200101/1/dfs_cdaaefb1-6698-11
eb-988d-4cedfb428a36_53486430_53797182.jpg?token=3caf4abd6e584013973602345c565072

3 API Interface 
All API interfaces of the system are based on the HTTP/1.1 protocol and follow the 
RESTFul style. All the interaction data is in JSON format. The version of the specific 
interface protocol is reflected by the interface URL. 
3.1 Login Authentication 
The VMS API can only be accessed after successful login authentication. The login 
authentication uses the secondary authentication process of Http Digest. The protocol is 
as follows. 
3.1.1 Trigger Authentication 
Brief Description 
• First login. Initiate the authentication process, the server will return the status 
code 401 Unauthorized and will provide random authentication information such 
as realm and randomKey in the response. 
Request URL 
• /brms/api/v1.0/accounts/authorize 
Request Method 
• POST 
Request Parameter 
• Body Parameters 
Parameter Required Type Description 
userName Yes string Username 
ipAddress No string Client computer IP address 
clientType No string Client type, write WINPC_V2 directly 
Request Example 
POST /brms/api/v1.0/accounts/authorize HTTP/1.1  
Dahua-HTTP-API-For-DSS-V8.7_EN for pt_era_baru_digitama

--- PAGE 21 ---
 
20 
 
Host: 192.168.1.1  
Connection: close  
Content-Type: application/json;charset=UTF -8 
 
{ 
    "userName": "system",  
    "ipAddress":    "",  
    "clientType": "WINPC_V2"  
} 
Return Parameter 
Parameter Type Description 
realm string Encrypted field. Used to generate a signature for the second login. 
randomKey string Random secret key. Can be used as a parameter for the second 
login and will take effect after 10 seconds. 
encryptType string Encryption mode. Can be used as a parameter for the second login. 
publickey string Platform RSA-encrypted public key, base64 coded. Can be used to 
encrypt the secret key and vector of the AES encryption algorithm. 
Return Example 
{ 
    "realm": "f689ed8c40030d68007d6e95002f7f87", 
    "randomKey": "48c008d0026a49c4", 
    "encryptType": "MD5", 
    "publickey": "MIGf000GCS...iH+FFwu9wID00AB" 
} 
3.1.2 Submit Credentials 
Brief description 
• Second login. For the procedure, see [5.1 Login Authentication]. A signature will 
be generated based on the authentication information returned from triggering 
the authentication process. You need to enter it into the request. The server will 
respond with a 200 OK status code and an access token. The random 
authentication information returned from triggering authentication is valid for 10 
seconds. Please submit the credentials within 10 seconds. 
Request Method 
• POST 
Request URL

signature Yes string 
Authentication data. The signature is 
calculated as follows: 
temp1 = md5(password) 
temp2 = md5(userName + temp1) 
temp3 = md5(temp2) 
temp4 = md5(userName + ":" + realm + ":" + temp3) 
signature = md5(temp4 + ":" + randomKey) 
userName Yes string Username 
randomKey Y es string 
Random value, returned from the interface in 
the first login and becoming invalid after 10 
seconds 
publicKey No string 
Terminal RSA public key, note not the 
platform's public key. Compatible with 
previous versions, it can now be directly 
transferred to empty. 
ipAddress No string IP address 
clientType No string Client type, write WINPC_V2 directly. 
userType No string User type: 0: System user; 1: Domain user. 0 by 
default. 
secretKey No string 
User encryption and decryption key, 
ciphertext = encryption(secret key, platform 
public key). Use 32-bit random string in 
plaintext before encryption. 
secretVector No string 
User encryption and decryption vector, 
ciphertext = encryption(secret vector, 
platform public key). Use 16-bit random string 
in plaintext before encryption 
loginType 否 string Login type: 1 = normal login, 2 = multi-site 
login, default 1 
Request Example 
Dahua-HTTP-API-For-DSS-V8.7_EN for pt_era_baru_digitama

--- PAGE 23 ---
 
22

Connection: close  
Content-Type: application/json;charset=UTF -8

Parameter Type Description

userName 
string Username

- amqp string Amqp protocol address

- wss string Wss protocol address

- password string 
The password, after AES encryption, needs to be decrypted using the 
secret key secretKey and vector secretVector returned by [3.1.2 
Submit Credentials]. For the decryption method, refer to the 
decryptWithAES7 method in [6.4 Encryption and Decryption 
Example]. Among them, the secretKey and the secretVector are not 
clear text, but are encrypted by RSA and can only be used after 
decryption. For the decryption method, refer to the 
decryptRSAByPrivateKey method in [6.4 Encryption and Decryption 
Example].

- - week string Week (the field value is 0 for the date 
mode); -1 means the final week 
- - day string Date (meaning a weekday in the 
week mode); 0 means Sunday 
- - time string Time, such as 09:30 
- dstEndTime object End time of DST 
- - month string Month 
- - week string Week (the field value is 0 for the date 
mode); -1 means the final week 
- - day string Date (meaning a weekday in the 
week mode); 0 means Sunday 
- - time string Time, such as 09:30 
- timeSyncStatus string 
Syncing status: 0 = Failed; 1 = 
Successful; 2 = In distribution; 3 = 
Not supported

- - name string Name 
- - property string Unidirection/Bidirection information

stream: 0 = No; 1 = Yes

3.3.1.2 Get the List of Devices in Pages 
Brief Description 
• Get list of devices in pages. Calling interfaces requires administrator privileges. 
Request Method 
• GET 
Request URL 
• /brms/api/v1.1/device/page 
Dahua-HTTP-API-For-DSS-V8.7_EN for pt_era_baru_digitama

--- PAGE 56 ---
 
55 
 
Request Parameters 
• Body Parameters 
Parameter Required Type Description 
page Yes string Page number, staring from 1, the maximum value 
is 2147483647 
pageSize Yes string Number of entries each page, staring from 1, the 
maximum value is 10000 
orderType No string 
Sorting type: 1 = device IP,2 = device model, 3 = 
device code. If it is null, default sorting by online 
status 
orderDirection No string Sorting direction: 0 = Ascending sequence; 1 = 
Descending sequence, default 1 
keyword No string Keywords, fuzzy search supported, to match 
device name, IP, and device code 
orgCode No string Organization code 
deviceCategory No string Device category 
deviceType No string Device sub-category 
status No string Device status: 0 = Offline; 1 = Online; null means 
all 
permitted No string Permission filtering: 0 = Not filtered; 1 = Filtered; 
null means all 
domain No s tring Cascade device included or not: 0 = No; 1 = Yes; 
null means all 
sourceType No s tring Device channel type: 1=Platform, 3= Third-party, 
blank indicates querying all 
containChild No string Include subsets: 0=No, 1=Yes, default to 1 
protocolTypes No s tring 
Protocol type: 1=Dahua Protocol, 2=Hikvision 
Access, 99=Onvif Access, 185=Jiuzhou Protocol, 
multiple separated by commas, empty indicates 
all 
manufacturers No s tring 
Manufacturer: 1=Dahua, 2=Hikvision, 4=AXIS, 
5=Uniview, 6=BOSCH, 185=JIUZHOU, 
246=Other, multiple separated by commas, 
empty means query all 
Request Example 
GET /brms/api/v1.1/device/page?page=1&pageSize=20&orderType=&orderDirection=
&orgCode=001&deviceCategory=&deviceType=&status=&keyword=&permitted=&do
main=&sourceType=&containChild=&protocolTypes=&manufacturers= HTTP/1.1 
Host: 192.168.1.1

Type]

Request parameter 
• Body Parameters

data Yes object None

Keyboard code; if the parameter channel

code

and video

- fakeSdp No string Forge SDP or not: 0 = No, 1 = Yes,

3.4.2 Start Talk 
Brief Description 
• Start talk. The usage method is similar to that of real-time video. You also need to 
splice url and token. Please refer to the 7.1.2 section. 
Request Method 
• POST 
Request URL 
• /brms/api/v1.0/MTS/Audio/StartTalk 
Request Parameter 
• Body Parameters 
Parameter Required Type Description 
data Yes object None 
- channelSeq No string Channel sequence (used for channel talk), 
the maximum value is 1024 
- 
broadcastChannels 
No string Broadcast channels ( used for broadcast talk) 
- deviceCode Yes string Device code 
- talkType Yes string Talk type: 1-Device, 2-Channel, 3- National 
standard device broadcast 
- audioType No string Audio type: 0-DEFAULT, 1-PCM, 2-G711a, 3-
AMR, 4-G711u, 5-G726… 
- talkMode No string 
Talk mode: 0-Talk (Default mode), 1-
Broadcast (switching from broadcasting to 
intercom requires reconfiguration) 
Dahua-HTTP-API-For-DSS-V8.7_EN for pt_era_baru_digitama

--- PAGE 87 ---
 
86 
 
Parameter Required Type Description 
- audioBit Yes string Represent with actual values. If it is 8 digits, 
the value is 8 
- sampleRate No string The sampling rate, such as 16k, has a value 
of 16000 
- enableRtsps No string Whether to enable RTSPS: 0 = disabled, 1 = 
enabled, default 0 
Request Example 
POST /brms/api/v1.0/MTS/Audio/StartTalk HTTP/1.1  
Host: 192.168.1.1  
Connection: close  
Content-Type: application/json;charset=UTF -8

        "audioBit": "16",

        "enableRtsps": "0"  
    } 
}

Parameter Type Description

desc string Result description 
data object None 
- deviceCode string Device code 
- url string RTSP address. It is mutually exclusive with VDTS IP/Port 
- token string RTSP token 
- session string Talk session 
- audioType string 
If the audioType supported by the client request is available, it will 
be used as is. Otherwise, the audio will be sent in the following 
order of priority: G711a, G711u, PCM, G726, AMR, DEFAULT. If 
Dahua-HTTP-API-For-DSS-V8.7_EN for pt_era_baru_digitama

--- PAGE 88 ---
 
87 
 
Parameter Type Description 
none of these audio types are supported by the device, the first 
available audioType provided by the device will be selected 
- audioBit string Represent with actual values. If it is 8 digits, the value is 8 
- sampleRate string The sampling rate, such as 16k, has a value of 16000 
- 
protocolType 
string Protocol type version

3.6 Alarm(Event Center) 
3.6.1 Subscribe to Alarms 
Brief Description 
• Subscribe alarm, push alarm information through callback, the requester needs to 
define the callback interface according to the specified protocol. The same user 
only supports subscribing once, and repeating the subscription will overwrite the 
results of the previous subscription. 
• An alarm message might require multiple callbacks to complete, usually no more 
than 2. The structure of multiple callbacks is the same, and the message type is 
distinguished by the callbackType field. When callbackType=1, it is the main 
content of the alarm message, and all fields need to be paid attention to, 
including alarmPictures (the image address carried by the alarm itself); when 
callbackType=2, it is the linked image information, usually the asynchronous 
obtained alarm linkage image, at this time, only alarmCode and alarmPictures 
need to be updated, other fields should not be updated, otherwise the original 
Dahua-HTTP-API-For-DSS-V8.7_EN for pt_era_baru_digitama

--- PAGE 102 ---
 
101 
 
alarm information will be cleared. It should be noted that when updating 
alarmPictures, the increment method should be used, otherwise it will overwrite 
the image carried by the original alarm itself.  
Callback format:  
POST callbackUrl HTTP/1.1  
Content-Type: application/json;charset=UTF -8) 
{ 
"callbackType": "Callback message type: 1 = alarm message body, 2 = linked imag
e (usually asynchronously obtained alarm linkage image, in this case only the alar
mPictures field needs to be incremented), default 1, required",  
"alarmCode": "Alarm code, required",  
"sourceCode": "Alarm source code, required",  
"sourceName": "Alarm source name, optional",  
"alarmType": "Alarm type code, required",  
"alarmTypeName": "Alarm type name, optional",  
"alarmGrade": "Alarm level: 1=High, 2=Medium, 3=Low, required",  
"alarmStatus": "Alarm status: 1=Alarm gene rated, 2=Alarm cleared, required",  
"alarmTime": "Alarm time, timestamp, required",  
"alarmPictures": [  
    "Alarm image, Base64 encoding, optional"  
], 
"remark": "Alarm scheme remarks, optional",  
"eventRemark": "Alarm event remarks, optional",  
"extData": "Ex tended data, in JavaScript Object Notation (JSON) format, may contai
n some business -related information. The data structure may vary depending on th
e business, optional.",  
"signature": "Signature data, optional"  
} 
Request Method 
• POST  
Request URL 
• /brms/api/v1.1/push-data/alarm/subscribe 
Request Parameter 
• Body Parameters 
Parameter Required Type Description 
callbackUrl Yes string Callback address, supports http and https 
action Yes string Action: 1 = subscribe, 0 = unsubscribe 
signature No string Signature data, carried during callback, can be used for 
authentication, empty means callback interface does 
Dahua-HTTP-API-For-DSS-V8.7_EN for pt_era_baru_digitama

--- PAGE 103 ---
 
102 
 
Parameter Required Type Description 
not require authentication. The format is determined 
by the requester, generally using a random string is 
sufficient. 
Request Example 
POST /brms/api/v1.1/push-data/alarm/subscribe HTTP/1.1  
Host: 192.168.1.1  
Connection: close  
Content-Type: application/json;charset=UTF -8 
X-Subject-Token: 26aa1095c9364d6b94be425d5b8798b7  
 
{ 
    "callbackUrl": "https://192.168.1.1:443/brms/api/v1.1/push -data/alarm/push", 
    "action": "1",

}

Brief Description 
• Obtain access control records by page. The obtained records are used for

• POST

• /obms/api/v1.1/acs/access/record/fetch/page 
Request Parameter 
• Body Parameters 
Parameter Required Type Description 
page Yes string Page number, staring from 1, the 
maximum value is 2147483647 
pageSize Yes string Number of entries each page, staring 
from 1, the maximum value is 10000 
channelIds No array The channel code 
alarmTypeIds No array Alarm type id. Dictionary type, see 
[6.1.7 Alarm Type] 
personId No string The personnel ID. Exact search is 
supported. 
startTime Yes string The start time (in seconds) 
Dahua-HTTP-API-For-DSS-V8.7_EN for pt_era_baru_digitama

--- PAGE 181 ---
 
180 
 
Parameter Required Type Description 
endTime Yes string The end time (in seconds) 
currentPage No string 
The current page number, used when 
flipping pages, helps to turn pages 
faster 
splitId No string 
Page splitting ID, when flipping up, it is 
the ID of the first record, and when 
flipping down, it is the ID of the last 
record. Used when flipping, it helps to 
flip pages faster 
splitTime No string 
Page splitting timestamp, when 
flipping up, it is the time of the first 
record, and when flipping down, it is 
the time of the last record. Timestamp 
(in seconds), used when flipping, helps 
to flip pages faster

3.11.3.5 Get the Snapshot Records of Vehicles at the Entrance and Exit in Pages 
Brief Description

• POST  
Request URL 
• /ipms/api/v1.1/entrance/vehicle-capture/record/fetch/page

Parameter Required Type Description

search

car 
vehicleColor No string Vehicle color, dictionary type, see [API 
Reference > Dictionary > Vehicle Color] 
vehicleModel No string Vehicle model, dictionary type, see [API 
Reference > Dictionary > Vehicle Model] 
endTime Yes string Search end time, timestamp (seconds) 
entranceGroupId No string Vehicle entrance and exit group ID 
personName No string Owner name, which supports fuzzy 
search 
channelIds No array Channel code 
orgCode No string Person group ID 
startTime Yes string Search start time, timestamp (seconds)

maximum value is 2147483647 
Dahua-HTTP-API-For-DSS-V8.7_EN for pt_era_baru_digitama

--- PAGE 275 ---
 
274 
 
Parameter Required Type Description 
pageSize Yes string Number of entries each page, staring 
from 1, the maximum value is 10000 
vehicleBrand No string Vehicle brand, dictionary type, see [API 
Reference > Dictionary > Vehicle Brand] 
currentPage No string The current page number, used when 
flipping pages, helps to turn pages faster 
splitId No string 
Page splitting ID, when flipping up, it is 
the ID of the first record, and when 
flipping down, it is the ID of the last 
record. Used when flipping, it helps to 
flip pages faster 
splitTime No string 
Page splitting timestamp, when flipping 
up, it is the time of the first record, and 
when flipping down, it is the time of the 
last record. Timestamp (in seconds), used 
when flipping, helps to flip pages faster

Brief Description

• POST  
Request URL

Request Parameters  
• Body Parameters 
Parameter Required Type Description 
countType Y es s tring 
Statistics Type: 1 = day, 2 = week, 3 = 
month, Required. When countType is 2, the 
start date of each week will be entered (that 
is the date of Sunday), such as: 2022-09-11, 
when countType is 3, only month will be 
entered, such as: 2022-09 
countDate No s tring Date of the counting, format: YYYY-MM-DD, 
Required 
startDate No string Statistics start date, format: YYYY-MM-DD, 
required when countType = 4 
endDate No string Statistics end date, format: YYYY-MM-DD, 
required when countType = 4 
parkingLotIds No array Parking lot ID, empty means all the parking 
lots

3.11.4.6 Remote Opening 
Brief Description 
• Remote opening. For opening results, see the MQ massage: [4.6.4 Notification of 
Snapshot Information of Vehicles at the Entrance and Exit]. Configure parameters 
as needed for specific scenarios. If it is only for the purpose of opening the gate, 
the general parameters can be set to blank or default values. 
Request Method 
Dahua-HTTP-API-For-DSS-V8.7_EN for pt_era_baru_digitama

• Body Parameters 
Parameter Required Type Description

When the identified license 
plate is found to be incorrect, 
correct the license plate and 
the platform will 
synchronously modify 
theentry or exit records 
correctTime No string Time correction (second) 
forceRecapture  
N
o string 
Is it mandatory to retake the 
image when the identified 
license plate is found to be 
incorrect: 1=Yes, 0=No, 
default to 0 
parkingSpaceStat
isticsType 
No string 
Remainder calculation rules: 
1=calculated, 2=not 
calculated, 3=calculated 
according to configuration 
rules, default to 3 
saveRecord No string Save entry/exit records: 
1=Yes, 0=No, default to 1

3.12.2.4 Face Snapshot Records — Search by Image (Download Image) 
Brief Description 
• Face snapshot record—Search by picture (download picture). The picture URL 
obtained from the original IVSS device is a relative path on the device, and you 
should manually download the picture (up to 10 pictures in each request) to store 
it into the OSS. Download is not required subsequently. 
Request Method 
• POST 
Request URL 
• /brms/api/v1.1/face/detection/record/device/picture/download 
Request Parameter 
• Body Parameters 
Parameter Required Type Description 
session Yes string Search by picture, session mark 
deviceCode Yes string Device number 
urls Yes object None 
- id Yes string Record ID 
- type Yes string Record picture type: 1 = Face 
picture; 2 = Scenario picture

3.13.4 Downloading a Captured Body Image. 
Brief Description 
• Download a captured body image. If an image is obtained from the IVSS device of 
an earlier version, the image URL is a relative path. In this case, you must 
download the image again. Then, the image can be stored to OSS, and you do 
not need to download the image in the future. 
Request Method 
• POST 
Request URL 
• /brms/api/v1.1/video-analyse/human/record/device/picture/download 
Request Parameter 
• Body Parameters 
Parameter Required Type Description 
deviceCode Yes string The device number, required. 
urls Yes object None 
- id Yes string The record ID, required. 
- type Yes string 
The type of the recorded 
image, required: 1 = Face 
image, 2 = Scene image, 3 = 
Body image. 
- url Yes string The URL of the recorded 
image, required. 
Dahua-HTTP-API-For-DSS-V8.7_EN for pt_era_baru_digitama

the ID of the last record when 
you scroll down a page. This 
parameter is required when 
you scroll up or down a page.

time

1 = Descending 
direction No string 
Movement direction, 0 = 
unknown, 1 = A->B direction, 
2 = B->A direction, 3 = A->B 
and B->A direction

4 MQ Notification Message 
Public Message Protocol is received by all users, whereas Private Message Protocol is only 
sent to the specified users with the themes distinguished by the user ID. 
4.1 Device

Parameter Type Description 
method string The method name. 
info object None

- onlineStatus string The status: 0 = Offline, 1 = Online. 
- offlineReason string The offline reason. 
- syncChannelStauts string 
Whether to synchronize the channel 
status: 0 =  No, 1  =  Yes. The default 
value is 1. 
- updateTime string The change interval, in seconds.

5 Best Practices 
5.1 Login Authentication 
 
Developers get the username and password of VMS and log in to the platform using 
HTTP Digest authentication. After successful login authentication, they can obtain the 
identity credential ‘token’ and the ‘credential’ information for accessing platform images 
or files. For security reasons, the token is valid for 30 seconds by default. Developers need 
to call the heartbeat keep-alive interface once within 30 seconds to keep the token alive. 
The validity period of the token is 30 minutes. Developers need to call the update token 
interface once within 30 minutes to refresh the Token. For security reasons, VMS 
separates the access API credential (Token) and the access image credential (Credential). 
Credential does not need to be kept alive or updated separately. When updating the 
token, VMS will synchronously associate and update the credential. 
Login Authentication Process: 
 
Dahua-HTTP-API-For-DSS-V8.7_EN for pt_era_baru_digitama

--- PAGE 503 ---
 
502 
 
Docking Example: 
See [6.3 Docking Example]. 
5.1.1 Get Authentication Token 
Step1 First authentication For specific parameters, see the [3.1.1 Trigger Authentication] 
interface 
For the first authentication request, carry the userName. The platform then returns Error 
Code 401 (meaning no permission), and contains encrypted information (including realm, 
randomKey, encryptType and publickey) in the message body. 
Step 2 Second authentication For specific parameters, see the [3.1.2 Submit Credentials] 
interface. 
The requester generates a pair of AES secret key (32-bit string) and vector (16-bit string), 
and encrypts them using the RSA public key (publickey) returned by the first login. The 
second authentication request needs to use the encrypted AES secret key and vector, and 
use base64 encoding as parameters. Pseudocode examples: 
aesSecretKey = UUID.replace(" -", "");  
aesSecretVector = UUID.replace(" -", "").substring(16);  
encryptedAesSecretKeyWithBase64 = Base64(encryptByPublicKey(aesSecr etKey, Base64(fi rstLoginRetu
rnPublickey))); 
encryptedAesSecretVectorWithBase64 = Base64(encryptByPublicKey(aes SecretVector, Base64(firstLogi
nReturnPublickey))); 
In the second authentication, user requests shall carry the signature. The signature is 
calculated with the userName, password, realm, randomKey in the following way: 
Pseudocode examples: 
temp1 = md5(password)  
temp2 = md5(userName + temp1)  
temp3 = md5(temp2)  
temp4 = md5(userName + ":" + realm + ":" + temp3)  
signature = md5(temp4 + ":" + randomKey)  
As shown in the aforementioned pseudocodes, a total of 5 times of MD5 encryption is 
needed. The parameter values and results values are all character strings. The result value 
of MD5 encryption are all in lower case, and the length of MD5 encryption is 32 digits. 
The assumed values are as follows: 
Calculated values at each stage are as follows: 
Parameter Value 
userName "system" 
password "admin123" 
realm "VMS" 
randomKey "9c2b603650f54bcb" 
Dahua-HTTP-API-For-DSS-V8.7_EN for pt_era_baru_digitama

--- PAGE 504 ---
 
503 
 
Times of 
encryption Parameter/Result Value 
1 Parameter "admin123" 
1 Result "0192023a7bbd73250516f069df18b500" 
2 Parameter "system0192023a7bbd73250516f069df18b500" 
2 Result "5a0fdbe44b86807b5e5e127918bbc475" 
3 Parameter "5a0fdbe44b86807b5e5e127918bbc475" 
3 Result "1e27fadce9af09e120ab5142a83a679e" 
4 Parameter "system:VMS:1e27fadce9af09e120ab5142a83a679e"

5 Parameter "4b923d65cbbfd724285a164c3178b055:9c2b603650f54bcb" 
5 Result "024a3dc397a3844bb31d24f22b4d6035" 
In the case of a domain user, the signature algorithm is different. signature = RSA 
(password, platform public key). The platform public key is the same publickey returned in 
the first login. 
Two times of login authentication shall be completed in 10 seconds. Otherwise, the 
randomKey returned from the first authentication interface becomes invalid, and the 
interface returns Error Code 1101 (The nonce is illegal.) Therefore, using tools like 
Postman to commission the login authentication interface one by one is not 
recommended. Instead, coding shall be used to quickly complete two login requests. 
5.1.2 Token Keepalive 
For specific parameters, see the [3.1.3 Heartbeat Keep-alive] interface. 
After successful authentication, the heartbeat keeping interface shall be called for keep-
alive during keep-alive period. The keep-alive interval is recommended to be 2/3 of the 
keep-alive lasting period (every 20 seconds).The keep-alive request needs to bring the 
current valid authentication token. The token value is put in the X-Subject-Token 
parameter of the request head, and null is passed to the request message body. 
5.1.3 Update Token 
For specific parameters, see the [3.1.4 Update Token] interface. 
After successful authentication, although the token starts keeping alive, it remains invalid 
after tokenRate. Therefore, you need to call the update token interface to get a new 
token, and keep alive with it. It is recommended that the interval for updating token is 2/3 
of tokenRate. If the tokenRate is 1,800, it means that the period of validity is 30 minutes, 
and the token update frequency is about 20 minutes. After token update, to ensure 
consistent request authentication, the old token will be deleted in one minute. 
5.1.4 Cancel Token Authorization 
Dahua-HTTP-API-For-DSS-V8.7_EN for pt_era_baru_digitama

--- PAGE 505 ---
 
504 
 
For specific parameters, see the [3.1.5 Logout] interface.  
Logout on the client requires calling the authorization cancellation interface, and null is 
passed to the request message body.

5.2 Device Management 
 
After the developer successfully logs in to the VMS platform, he can use the token to 
obtain resource information (organization, device, channel).Getting the device tree 
involves two protocols: Device organization tree and device list. 
1. The device tree can get the relative relations of all organizations, devices, and 
channels. 
2. The device list gets detailed information (such as device IP, port, and type) of devices, 
units, and channels. 
Channel coding rules: 
A channel code consists of the device code (deviceCode), unit type (unitType), unit 
number (unitSeq), and channel number (channelSeq), separated by $. See the figure 
below:  
Dahua-HTTP-API-For-DSS-V8.7_EN for pt_era_baru_digitama

--- PAGE 506 ---
 
505 
 
 
Where The deviceCode is a 7-digit number. The device code of the newly added device 
on the platform increases one by one, starting from 1000000. The unitType see [6.1.3 Unit 
Type]. For detailed meanings, see the table below. The unitSeq represents the unit 
number that starts from 0. The channelSeq represents the channel number that starts 
from 0. In the figure above, 1000000$1$0$3 means the 4th channel of the 1st unit of the 
coding unit of the device whose deviceCode is 1000000. If it is a subordinate device, the 
device code is like 1000000@001. This format indicates that the device comes from a 
cascaded domain with code 001, and the device code on the lower level platform is 
1000000. 
5.2.1 Getting Device Details 
Search the device details on the platform through the device code. 
5.2.2 Getting list of devices in pages 
Get list of devices in pages. 
5.2.3 Device Organization Tree (All) 
 
Multiple organizations and devices can be loaded under an organization. Units of 
different types can be loaded under a device. Multiple channels can be loaded under a 
unit. The device tree interface supports conditional search by channel type (channelTypes) 
and organization (orgCode). 
The organization tree established through the returned data by request. This organization 
tree has devices and channels, but no specific information of them. The specific 
information needs to be obtained from the device list. 
Dahua-HTTP-API-For-DSS-V8.7_EN for pt_era_baru_digitama

--- PAGE 507 ---
 
506 
 
5.2.4 Device Organization Tree (Graded) 
Sometimes there are too many devices to be all displayed each time, so they can be 
displayed by grade. For this purpose, search child nodes (excluding grand child nodes) 
that meet conditions according to the parent node ID. The root node can be searched for 
null transmission. The subordinate level of an organization can be either organizations or 
devices. The subordinate level of devices can only be channels which have no subordinate 
levels.

5.3 Video Services 
5.3.1 Overall Solution of Video Playing 
For complex video services, the VMS supports various playback protocols (RTSP/FLV/HLS) 
tailored to different application scenarios. To facilitate development, VMS also provides 
various development kits (browser plugins/PC SDK/App SDK), allowing developers to 
choose the appropriate integration method based on their specific use cases.

5.3.2 Application Scenarios and Recomended Solutions 
 Recommended solutions for video playback in web browsers:  
Integrate browser playback plugins or use FLV/HLS protocols for plugin-free video 
playback. Note that both FLV and HLS protocols do not support H.265 (HEVC) encoded 
streams by default.  
 Recomended Solution for PC Client: 
Integrate DPSDK or directly utilize RTSP/RTSPS protocols to enable video preview, 
recording playback, video downloads, and additional functionalities. 
 Recomended Solution for App: 
Integrate Android/iOS DPSDK or directly utilize RTSP/RTSPS protocols to enable video 
preview, recording playback, video downloads, and additional features. 
 Recomened Solution for third-party player such as VLC or third-party pull stream 
service: 
There is no need to login to the VMS platform; Use RTSP redirection to pull stream 
directly. In this mode, the RTSP URL remains valid indefinitely, eliminating token 
expiration issues. For third-party developers needing to persistently save stream 
addresses, we recommend utilizing RTSP redirection, directly pulling streams by 
redirecting to the platform's media gateway (MGW) on port 9090. 
Dahua-HTTP-API-For-DSS-V8.7_EN for pt_era_baru_digitama

5.3.4 Introduction of Pulling Stream Methods 
 The playing process based on browser plugins: 
VMS provides a web plug-in JavaScript SDK for browser users. This SDK encapsulates the 
RTSP over WebSocket pulling stream process, supports H.264/H.265 decoding, and allows 
for real-time playback and replay functions. The integration steps are as follows: 
1) The developer contacts the VMS marketing representative to obtain the web plugin's 
JavaScript package. 
2) The developer interacts with the VMS platform via the REST API to retrieve video 
channel information. 
3) The developer integrates the web plugin package to play video or recordings from a 
specified video channel. 
 The playing process based on DPSDK: 
VMS provides the DPSDK dynamic library (DLL) for use in PC clients and apps. The DLL 
encapsulates the RTSP pulling stream process, enabling the implementation of complex 
video functionalities such as live video, playback, and intercom by integrating the DLL. 
The steps are as follows: 
1) The developer contacts the VMS marketing department representative to obtain the 
DPSDK dynamic library. 
Dahua-HTTP-API-For-DSS-V8.7_EN for pt_era_baru_digitama

--- PAGE 510 ---
 
509 
 
2) The developer interacts with the VMS platform through the REST API to obtain video 
channel information. 
3) The developer calls the DPSDK dynamic library to play the video or recording of a 
specified video channel. 
 The playing process based on FLV/HLS: 
FLV/HLS are popular audio and video streaming protocols for browsers that enable 
plugin-free playing. VMS supports FLV/HLS pulling stream; however, these services are 
not included by default in the VMS baseline package. To enable FLV/HLS pulling stream, 
please contact the sales team to obtain the service. Once installed on the VMS platform, it 
will be supported. 
The steps are: 
o The developer contacts the VMS sales department to obtain the FLV/MES service 
package and installs it on the VMS platform. 
o The developer interacts with the VMS platform through the REST API to obtain video 
channel resources. 
o The developer uses the REST API to request the FLV/HLS pulling stream URL for the 
specified video resource from the VMS. 
o The developer implements real-time video preview using FLV and video playback 
using HLS. 
 FLV URL format: 
http://[service IP]:[service port]/live/cameraid/[camera ID]/substream/[stream type]/files.flv  
For example: https://172.7.2.110:7896/live/cameraid/1000000%240/substream/1.flv 
 HLS URL format: 
Central recording playback: 
http://[service IP]:[service port]/vod/center/cameraid/[camera ID]/substream/[stream 
type]/recordtype/recording type/totallength/[actual recording time]/begintime/[begin 
time]/endtime/[end time].m3u8 
Device recording playback: 
http://[ service IP]:[ service port]/vod/device/cameraid/[ camera ID D]/substream/[ stream 
type]/recordtype/recording type/totallength/[ actual recording time]/begintime/[start 
time]/endtime/[end time].m3u8 
 Parameter description: 
[service IP]: The IP address of the server hosting the MES. If the MES is deployed 
Dahua-HTTP-API-For-DSS-V8.7_EN for pt_era_baru_digitama

--- PAGE 511 ---
 
510 
 
in a distributed manner, the IP is that of the server where the MESGW service is 
located.  
[service port]: The port that the MES service listens on is 7086 by default. If the 
MES is deployed in a distributed manner, the port will be that of the MESGW 
service. 
[camera ID]: such as 1000000%40001%240. 1000000 represents the device 
number, and 001 represents the cascade number. The two are separated by "%40," 
which represents "@". "%24" represents the symbol "$", and the trailing "0" 
indicates channel 1 (starting from 0). 
[stream type]: 1 represents the main stream and 2 represents the auxiliary stream. 
[actual recording time]: The actual total recording time obtained from SS. The unit 
is second. 
[recording type]: central recording: recordType=0 all, recordType=1 general 
recording,  recordType=2 alarm recording, recordType=81  
supplementary record, recordType=82 alarm pre-recording 
device recording: recordType=0 all, recordType=2 alarm recording, recordType=3 
motion detection, recordType=6 general recording 
[begin time] and [end time]: The start and end times of the recording, 
represented as int. The unit is second. 
 The playing process based on RTSP redirection: 
Developers often do video streaming tests based on VLC tools. The advantage of using 
RTSP redirection is that they can pull streams without logging in to the VMS platform. 
Developers can assemble URLs according to the RTSP format required by VMS, and can 
directly assemble username and passwords into RTSP addresses. If they do not know the 
username and passwords, they can also open the RTSP allowlist on the VMS platform 
(System Configuration-> Security-> RTSP AllowList Configuration) to add the address of 
the pull stream to the allowlist. They can also pull the stream, and the URL of the pull 
stream is not valid for a long time, and there is no Token expiration problem. 
 RTSP URL format of VMS pulling stream: 
rtsp://username:password@platform 
IP:9090/dss/monitor/params?cameraid=1000004%240&substream=1&username="usern
ame" 
Dahua-HTTP-API-For-DSS-V8.7_EN for pt_era_baru_digitama

--- PAGE 512 ---
 
511 
 
Note: Request the real-time video from the VMS for the 1000004$0 channel (where 
1000004 is the device code, %24 is the escape character for $, and 0 is the channel 
number) for the main stream (substream: 1 for main stream, 2 for substream). 
 RTSP URL format of VMS recording playback is as follows: 
rtsp://username: password@platfrom 
IP:9090/playback?cameraid=1000499%240&type=3&begintime=1602227183&endtime=
1602227192&substream=1&recordType=1&username="username" 
Note: Request the VMS media gateway for the 1000499$0 channel (where %24 is the 
escape character for $) for the main stream (substream: 1 for main stream, 2 for 
substream) of the ordinary recording (recordType: 1 for ordinary recording, 2 for alarm 
recording) with a start timestamp of 1602227183 and an end timestamp of 1602227192. 
 The playing process based on standard RTSP: 
After getting the RTSP address from the platform through the interface, the RTSP 
interaction process is supported: Starting from the OPTIONS signaling, the standard 
signaling process is adopted. A standard decoding library is used for decoding and 
playing. The platform only outputs streams. Functions like decoding, play, fast forward, 
and download are controlled by the play components, or to interface with the platform's 
DPSDK.
 
 Live View 
 
Requesting for live video has two steps: 
1. Get the playing URL and token through the Rest request. 
2. Get stream on URL through RTSP. 
Get URL 
Get the URL and token through the [3.4.1 Start Real-time Video] interface. The returned 
URL and token field will be used in subsequent RTSP interaction process. 
RTSP Interaction 
When sending a video request, the token field shall be used as the URL parameter. 
Without the token, the video request might fail. A token becomes invalid once it is 
used, or if it is not used after 30 seconds. The format of URL with token is shown as 
follows: 
rtsp://192.168.1.1:9100/vms/monitor/param/cameraid=1000002%240%26substream=1?token=1190 
Dahua-HTTP-API-For-DSS-V8.7_EN for pt_era_baru_digitama

--- PAGE 513 ---
 
512 
 
Standard RTSP acquire stream is supported, and VLC can be used for verification. To do 
this set the network configuration of VLC to RTP over RTSP (for specific configuration 
steps, do an online search). Open the network stream, and enter the URL. The returned 
streams in this mode are standard streams. A standard decoding library can be selected 
on the client for decoding.

 Recording Playback 
Recording Search 
For the protocol format of recording search, see [3.5.1 Search Recording]. Based on 
different video storage sources, there are device recordings, and platform recordings 
(center recordings) which are stored in the storage space configured on the platform. 
Storage space can be configured for both the central platform and distributed platform. 
Center recordings produced during the period when the device is mounted to a platform 
are stored in the storage space of this platform. Device recordings are stored on the 
device, regardless of to which platform the device is mounted. 
The API protocol does not support video download. It is recommended to use DPSDK 
docking, or the caller can obtain the RTSP address of the video obtained through the API 
and implement the download function themselves. 
Platform Recording Search 
Dahua-HTTP-API-For-DSS-V8.7_EN for pt_era_baru_digitama

--- PAGE 515 ---
 
514 
 
Platform recordings are stored in the storage space configured by the SS service where 
the device is mounted. If the device ever changed the SS service where it is mounted, the 
platform recordings in the search period might be in storage space of different SS 
services. Therefore, when searching platform recordings, the center service searches 
recordings from all SS services. The search process ends after all SS services return the 
search results. The unit of the returned recordings is file. See the following:  
{ 
"channelId": "1000001$1$0$0",  
"recordSource": "3",  
"recordType": "6",  
"startTime": "1545840000",  
"endTime": "1545841800",  
"recordName": "{2db653e6 -40d2-4bce-9df6-d2609b96d9ae}", 
"fileLength": "737280",  
"planId": "0",  
"ssId": "1001",  
"diskId": "1545840000 -1545841800", 
"streamId": "18",  
"forgotten": "0"  
} 
Device Recording Search 
When searching device recordings, the center service searches recordings from all SS 
services where the device is mounted. The unit of the returned recordings is file. See the 
following: 
{ 
    "channelId": "1000012$1$0$0",  
    "recordSource": "2",  
    "recordType": "6",  
    "startTime": "1545926402",  
    "endTime": "1545926473",  
    "recordName": "0 -2-172108-12288-1545926402-1545926473", 
    "fileLength": "12288",  
    "planId": "0",  
    "ssId": "1002",  
    "diskId": "",  
    "streamId": "0",  
    "forgotten": "0"  
} 
To request for recording playback, first get the recording playback URL, and the recording 
stream through the RTSP. 
Get Recording Playback URL 
Playback by file is recommended for platform recordings, because recording files in a 
period might correspond to different SS services (if the device ever changed the SS 
service to which it is bound). Recording playback can only be controlled on the client. 
Play a recording first, and then request to play the next one. In this case, playing the 
recordings in a period requires multiple recording playback requests. Playback by time is 
Dahua-HTTP-API-For-DSS-V8.7_EN for pt_era_baru_digitama

--- PAGE 516 ---
 
515 
 
recommended for device recordings, because this mode requires only one recording 
playback request. For the request protocol format of recording playback by time, see 
[3.5.2 Video Playback by Time]. For the request protocol format of recording playback by 
file, see [3.5.3 Video Playback by File]. 
Video Request on the Playback URL through RTSP Interaction 
Platform Recording 
Standard RTSP acquire stream is supported, and VLC can be used for verification. To do 
this set the network configuration of VLC to RTP over RTSP (for specific configuration 
steps, do an online search). Open the network stream, and enter the URL. The returned 
streams in this mode are standard streams. A standard decoding library can be selected 
on the client for decoding. The URL format is: 
rtsp://{IP}:{Port}/playback/center?streamID={streamID}&beginTime={beginTime}&endTime={endTime} 
IP and Port correspond to the IP and Port in the recording playback URL obtained in the 
previous step. The streamID is the one in the record of requested recordings. The 
beginTime and endTime are the start time and end time of the recording to be played. 
The beginTime can be later than the start time but not the end time of the recording to 
be played. 
The specific interaction procedure is as follows:

Device Recording 
Standard RTSP acquire stream is supported, and VLC can be used for verification. To do 
this set the network configuration of VLC to RTP over RTSP (for specific configuration 
steps, do an online search). Open the network stream, and enter the URL. The returned 
streams in this mode are standard streams. A standard decoding library can be selected 
on the client for decoding. The URL format is: 
rtsp://{IP}:{Port}/vms/playback/pu?cameraid={cameraid}&begintime={begintime}&endtime={endtime}
&substream={substream} 
IP and Port correspond to the IP and Port in the recording playback URL obtained in the 
previous step. The cameraid consists of the device code and channel serial number in the 
channelId requested in the previous step. The escape character %24 of '$' shall be added 
between the device code and channel code, for example, if the channelId is 
1000012$1$2$3, the cameraid will be 1000012%243. The begintime and endtime are the 
start time and end time of the recording to be played. The beginTime can be later than 
the start time but not the end time of the recording to be played. substream indicates 
main stream and sub stream. 1: Main stream; 2: Sub stream 
The specific interaction procedure is as follows:

5.3.5 The Connection Procedure for Typical Applications: Video 
Playback 
1. Add a device installed with a video player from [Basic Config>Device>Add Device] on 
the VMS client. 
 
2. Start API connection. Firstly, perform login authentication, including first login, second 
login, heartbeat keepalive, and token update. For details, refer to [5.1 Login Authentication] 
or [6.3.1.1 Example of Login Authentication with Java] on Demo.  
All subsequent API invocations need to carry the token field returned during logi ning in 
the X-Subject-Token request header. 
 
3. Get all devices from API document through [3.3.2.1 Getting Device Tree (All)]. 
The API input parameter is simple enough to be unquestionable. 
The output parameter is complicatedly structured and can be simplified as follows: 
"devices": [  
    { 
        "code": "1000747",  
        "name": "NVR",  
        ... 
        "units": [  
            { 
                "unitType": "1",  
                ... 
                "channels": [  
                    { 
                        "channelCode": "1000747$1$0$0",  
                        ... 
                    } 
                ] 
            } 
        ] 
    } 
] 
Wherein, 
code: Indicates a unique device identifier, which can be displayed or ignore d in the action 
bar of the client device list.  
name: Indicates a device name. These two fields can be used to determine whether t he 
device is the desired one.  
unitType: Indicates a unit type. 1 indicates a video unit and other units are ignored.  
channelCode: Indicates a unique channel identifier. All stream pull actions are bas ed on 
channels. 
 
4. Get the video playback URL from API document through [3.4.1 Start Real-time Video].  
Focus on main parameters: 
"data": {  
    ... 
    "channelId": "1000040$1$0$0",  
    ... 
} 
Wherein,  
Dahua-HTTP-API-For-DSS-V8.7_EN for pt_era_baru_digitama

--- PAGE 521 ---
 
520 
 
channelId: Indicates a unique channel identifier, corresponding to the channelCo de 
returned by the [3.3.2.1 Getting Device Tree (All)]API.  
Check the return value of the API: 
"data": {  
    ... 
    "url": "rtsp://  192.168.1.1:9100/vms/monitor/param/cameraid=1000040%240%26substream=1", 
    ... 
    "token": "2204",  
    ... 
} 
Wherein,  
url: Indicates the RTSP address of the pull stream. Your access will be denied when t his 
address is directly used for pulling stream.  
token: Indicates a video service authentication token. The token different from  that of the 
platform becomes invalid after being used once or not used for more than 30 seconds.  
 
5. Assemble the return value of the [3.4.1 Start Real-time Video] to make a complete RTSP 
stream pull URL: rtsp://  
192.168.1.1:9100/vms/monitor/param/cameraid=1000040%240%26substream=1?token=
2204, and use VLC or other standard decoding libraries to play videos.

5.4 Access Control 
Dahua-HTTP-API-For-DSS-V8.7_EN for pt_era_baru_digitama

--- PAGE 522 ---
 
521 
 
 
An access control module can unlock and lock a single door, implement global control of 
normally open and normally closed doors, and zone management and access rule. Zone 
management and access rule configuration are not supported in API documentation 
5.4.1 Unlock and Lock a Single Door 
On the platform, click the remote unlock and remote lock buttons of the specified door 
channel to unlock and lock the access control channel. The interface [3.7.1 Unlock and 
Lock a Single Door] is called. After operations of the access control channel is successful, 
the platform reports the operation record notification of the access control channel 
through MQ (notification of batch access control records: brms.notifyAcsEvents), and 
reports the door status notification through MQ (notification of door status: 
vms.doorAccessStatus).  
The interaction process is as follows:  
 
5.4.2 Global Control of Normally Open and Normally Closed Doors 
This function is to select access control channels in batch, and then perform operations 
on the channels. For example, keep them normally open, normally closed and restore 
them.  
Dahua-HTTP-API-For-DSS-V8.7_EN for pt_era_baru_digitama

--- PAGE 523 ---
 
522 
 
5.4.3 Zone Management 
The platform supports operations such as adding, updating, deleting, querying lists, and 
querying details of zones. Access points are automatically generated based on access 
control/elevator control channels, and each zone can be associated with one or more 
access points. It supports configuring access rules based on zones and access points for 
authorization issuance. 
5.4.4 Access Rule 
The platform supports the addition, update, deletion, list query, and detail query 
operations of traffic rules. The passage rules are divided into ordinary rules and advanced 
rules. Ordinary rules support time templates and holiday plans, and can be associated 
with one or more zones and passage points, bound to one or more personnel, vehicle 
organizations, and personnel for authorization issuance. There are many types of 
advanced rules that support time templates and authorization distribution based on the 
dimensions of access points and personnel. 
Go to the following directory to view the detailed API interfaces 
API Interface Directory 
API Interface

+++ Unlock and Lock of a Single Door 
+++ Configuring the Global Status of Access Control and Elevator Control for Access 
Control Zones 
+++ Obtaining a List of Access Rules that Were Not Configured for Resources 
+++ Get Access Control Area List 
+++ Get the Access Point List of the Specified Area of Access Control by Paging 
+++ Get the Access Control Point Access Status 
Go to the following directory to view the detailed MQ notifications 
MQ Notice Directory

+++ Notification of Normally Open and Normally Closed Door Status 
5.5 Personnel Management 
Dahua-HTTP-API-For-DSS-V8.7_EN for pt_era_baru_digitama

--- PAGE 524 ---
 
523 
 
 
5.5.1 Configure Personnel Group 
A person group is an organization to which persons belong, and is required when you 
add or update persons. By default, the platform has a person group named "All Persons 
and Vehicles" (Organization code 001, cannot be deleted).  
Call the [3.8.1.4 Get the List of Person Groups] interface to get list of person groups.  
Call the [3.8.1.1 Add a Person Group] interface to add person groups.  
Call the [3.8.1.2 Update a Person Group] interface to update person groups.  
Call the [3.8.1.3 Delete a Person Group] interface to delete person groups.  
5.5.2 Configure Person 
Call the [3.8.2.4 Get the Details of a Person] interface to get details of individual persons.  
Call the [3.8.2.5 Get the List of Persons in Pages] interface to get list of persons in pages.  
Call the [3.8.2.6 Get the List of Persons in Pages (Brief Information)] interface to get list of 
persons (brief information).  
Call the [3.8.2.1 Add a Person] interface to add person information. After successfully 
adding person information, the platform sends a notice through MQ ([4.4.1 Notification 
of Batch Adding Persons]) for successfully adding person information.  
Call the [3.8.2.2 Update a Person] interface to modify person information. After 
successfully modifying person information, the platform sends a notice through MQ 
([4.4.2 Notification of Batch Updating Persons]) for successfully modifying person 
information.  
Call the [3.8.2.3 Batch Delete Persons of a Specified Persons Group] interface to delete 
persons by group. After successfully deleting person information, the platform sends a 
notice through MQ ([4.4.3 Notification of Batch Deleting Persons]) for successfully 
deleting persons. 
5.5.3 Exceptions in Person and Search Re-sending 
There are three types of exception information: Access control, face comparison, entrance 
and exit.  
After calling the [3.8.2.5 Get the List of Persons in Pages] interface, call the [3.8.2.7 Get the 
List of Exceptions in Sending Data of Persons] interface to obtain the exception 
information of a batch of personnel. Then call the [3.8.2.8 Resend the Persons with 
Exceptions in Sending Data] interface to resend the exception information of a batch of 
personnel. 
Dahua-HTTP-API-For-DSS-V8.7_EN for pt_era_baru_digitama

--- PAGE 525 ---
 
524 
 
5.5.4 Access Control Event 
When the user triggers unlocking by card, fingerprint, password, and face recognition on 
an access control device, the platform pushes these real-time access control events 
through MQ (brms.notifyAcsEvents) to the client. 
The platform supports searching for the access control records by specified criteria. Call 
the interface [3.8.3.1 Obtaining Access Control Records by Page] to search for the access 
control history records by period and person ID. 
 
5.5.5 The Connection Procedure for Typical Applications: Add a 
Person 
The entire step is quite complex, and various associated information needs to be 
configured on the VMS client first. However, these are optional and there is no related 
business to omit. You can explain them in two scenarios.

for others. The following is an example of the most concise parameters, without the need 
to issue any data, only the personId and firstName have been set:

Scene 2: Require authorization for face, vehicle, and other business operations 
If it is necessary to configure associated services for authorization, rel evant configuration 
information needs to be queried through the API, and the [ 3.8.2.1 Add a Person] interface 
needs to be used. 
1. Add access control/face recognition/entrance & exit device  from [Basic 
Config>Device>Add Device] on the VMS client. 
 
2. Add person groups from [Applications Config>Person and Vehicle Info>Person List] 
on the VMS client or skip this step. The default group ID is 001. 
 
3. Add access rule from [Applications Config>Person and Vehicle Info>Person List ], on 
the VMS client. Configure zones and access points.

Roughly, the following modules are involved. Please focus on main parameters:  
baseInfo: { Basic information } 
personId: Indicates a unique person identifier which can be customized and conta in up to 
30 alphanumeric characters.  
orgCode: Indicates a person group ID, corresponding to the orgCode returned by the 
[3.8.1.4 Get the List of Person Groups] API.  
facePictures: Indicates face pictures. A maximum of two pictures can be adde d. For 
requirements, refer to the description about picture frame when you add a person on t he 
VMS client. The list displays Base64-encoded picture files. The face recognition camera and 
some access control devices deliver only the first picture. Try to keep t he first picture in 
Dahua-HTTP-API-For-DSS-V8.7_EN for pt_era_baru_digitama

--- PAGE 531 ---
 
530 
 
high definition. The second picture is for assistance and can be a picture wit h a pe rson 
wearing a hat or mask. The second picture is only delivered by some devices.  
extensionInfo: { Extended information } 
nationalityId: Indicates a region ID. Default set: Unknown=9999.  
residentInfo: { Residence information } 
houseHolder: If video call service is unavailable, set: 0=no house owner.  
sipId: If video call service is unavailable, set: ""=null.  
userDefineFields:{ User defined information } 
Generally, setting an empty array is sufficient. 
authenticationInfo: { Access control authentication information } 
combinationPassword: Indicates a combined unlock password.  This can be used in 
combination with card and fingerprint according to door configurations and the password 
needs to be AES encrypted. For details, refer to [3.3.5 Example of Encryption mode].  
cardNo: Indicates a card number., up to 16 characters.  
fingerprints: Fingerprint data  is generally collected directly from the device, which is 
relatively complex. If you do not have it, you can set it: []. 
palmVeins: Palm vein data is generally collected directly from the device, which is relatively 
complex. If you do not have it, you can set it: [].  
accessInfo: { Access control information } 
accessType: Indicates a person type. General setting: 0=General guestUseTi mes: Indicates 
an allowed unlock attempt count for a guest. For non guests, set: 0.  
passageRuleIds: Indicates the list of access rule IDs to be authorized, corresponding to the 
id returned by the [ 3.7.3 Obtaining a List of Access Rules that Were Not Configured for 
Resources] API.  
faceComparisonInfo: { Face comparison information } 
faceComparisonGroupId: Indicates the list of face comparison group IDs, corresponding to 
the repositoryId returned by the [3.12.1.4 Get Face Comparison Group List in pages] API.  
entranceInfo: { Vehicle entrance/exit information } 
vehicles: Indicates the list of vehicles.  
parkingSpaceQuotas: Parking available parking array 
parkingLotId: Parking lot ID, corresponding to the ID returned by the [3.11.4.1 Get Parking 
Resource Tree] interface 
entranceGroups: Parking vehicle group array 
entranceGroupIds: Indicates the list of vehicle entrance/exit group IDs, corr esponding to 
the groupId returned by the [3.11.1.4 Get the List of Entrance and Exit Groups of Vehicles] 
API.

pictures will be sent to the face recognition camera, and the license plate will  be sent to 
the entrance camera. 
 
15. For access control services, unlock events will be reported to the platform. To get unlock 
events in real time, monitor the messaging component named ActiveMQ. For operation 
methods, refer to [4 MQ Notification Message] or [6.3.2.1 Example of MQ Connection with 
Java] on Demo.

5.6.1 Visitor Manage 
 Generate the QR Code Data and Card Number in the Visitor Pass Permit 
Generate the QR code data and card number in the visitor pass permit. See [3.9.5 
Generate the QR Code Data and Card Number in the Visitor Pass Permit]. 
 New Visitors' Visit Registration and Appointment Registration 
Used to add a new visitor. See [3.9.3 Add a New Visitor]. The visitor status is visit after visit 
registration and appointment after appointment registration. Here are the specific steps: 
Step 1: Add user information. 
Step 2: Add visitor information. 
Step 3: Send a notification of adding the visitor. See [4.5.1 Notification of Adding a 
Visitor]. 
 Appointed Visit Registration, On-site Visitor's Leaving Registration, 
Cancellation of Appointment, and Update of On-site Visitors/Appointments 
Update the visitors' information and status. See [3.9.4 Update a Visitor]. Here are the 
specific steps: 
Step 1: Search for the visitor by visitor ID. 
Step 2: Delete the visitor who have left or canceled the appointment. Otherwise, update 
the visitor information. 
Step 3: If the visitor is deleted in Step 2, the corresponding person information and visitor 
information will be deleted too. 
Step 4: After Step 3 is completed, send a notification of deleting the visitor. See [4.5.3 
Notification of Batch Deleting Visitors]. 
Step 5: If the visitor is updated in Step 2, the corresponding person information and 
visitor information will be updated too. 
Step 6: After Step 5 is completed, send a notification of updating the visitor. See [4.5.2 
Notification of Updating a Visitor]. 
 Sign off Expired Visitors 
Sign off the expired visitors immediately. See [3.9.8 Sign off Expired Visitors].

5.7 Attendance Management 
 
5.7.1 Description of Unified Attendance Configuration Rules 
Before using the attendance function, you need to configure the following rules on the 
platform client first: 
• Attendance check point 
Add an access control device and configure the access control channel as the 
attendance check point. 
• Attendance periods 
Add corresponding fixed and unfixed attendance periods as required. 
• Attendance check shifts 
Add corresponding attendance shifts as required. 
• Attendance check holiday plan 
Configure the attendance check holiday plan as required. 
• Shift management 
Shifts are required during non-holiday periods for check-in/out to be recorded 
into attendance check history. You can use department shift, person shift and 
temporary shift as required. The person shift and department shift use the 
overwriting mechanism, and the last configuration should prevail. 
• Description of holiday and shift priority 
When there are multiple shifts or holidays on the same day, the priority is as 
follows: Temporary shift > Holiday shift > Person/Department shift. 
5.7.2 Description of Record Search 
Person ID uses precise search and name uses fuzzy search.  
Card Swiping Records 
• The generation conditions are as follows: 
1. Swiping card within the valid check-in range of the fixed attendance is 
check-in, and swiping card within the valid check-out range is check-out. 
Other events are null.  
2. All events where the day is a day off or holiday are null.  
Dahua-HTTP-API-For-DSS-V8.7_EN for pt_era_baru_digitama

--- PAGE 536 ---
 
535 
 
3. Unfixed attendance check does not enable rounding half to even. The first 
card swiping is check in, and the subsequent card swipings before the 
latest check-out time are all check-out.  
4. Unfixed attendance check enables rounding half to even. The first card 
swiping is check-in, the second valid card swiping is outing, and the third 
valid card swiping is returning; this is a loop. Events during card swiping 
intervals are null. 
• Search in pages 
Search card swiping records in pages. 
Attendance Report 
• The generation conditions are as follows: 
1. Fixed attendance check: There are card swiping records within the check-
in or check-out range.  
2. There are card swiping records on days off or holidays.  
3. Unfixed attendance check: There is one or multiple card swiping records.  
4. If there is no card swiping record, for shifts that do not cross day, the 
records will be generated by the system on the second day; for shifts that 
cross day, the records will be generated by the system on the third day. 
• Search in pages 
Search for attendance reports in pages. 
Exception Records 
• The generation conditions are as follows: 
1. Fixed attendance: According to the configured rules, the conditions 
include late, leave early, unauthorized absence, forget to check in/out, late 
and forget to check in, late and leave early, forget to check out and leave 
early.  
2. Unfixed attendance check: According to the configured rules, the 
conditions include late, forget to check in/out, late and forget to check in.  
3. Fixed attendance check: If you did not check in/out within the valid range, 
the system will generate unauthorized absence records. For shifts that do 
not cross day, the records will be generated on the second day; for shifts 
that cross day, the records will be generated on the third day. 
• Search in pages 
Search exception records in pages. 
Overtime Records 
• The generation conditions are as follows: 
1. Fixed attendance check: Checking out N minutes after the configured time 
is considered as overtime.  
2. Days off or holidays are considered as overtime.  
3. Unfixed attendance: Exceeding the configured minimum overtime 
duration is considered as overtime.  
• Search in pages 
Search overtime records in pages. 
Dahua-HTTP-API-For-DSS-V8.7_EN for pt_era_baru_digitama

--- PAGE 537 ---
 
536 
 
Outing Records 
• The generation conditions are as follows: 
Unfixed attendance enables rounding half to even. The first card swiping is check-
in, the second valid card swiping is outing, and the third valid card swiping is 
returning; this is a loop. 
• Search in pages 
Search outing records in pages. 
Go to the following directory to view the detailed API interfaces 
API Interface Directory 
API Interface
