+++ Get Card Swiping Records in Pages 
+++ Search Attendance Reports in Pages 
+++ Search Exception Records in Pages 
+++ Search Overtime Records in Pages 
+++ Get Outing Records in Pages 
5.8 Entrance and Exit 
 
[Parking lot]: The unique name of a specified parking lot.  
[Position]: As a part of the parking lot, it can be understood as a gate of the parking lot, 
such as the north gate. The position name must be unique in one parking lot.  
[Gate]: As a part of the position, it can be understood as a barrier arm. It is the minimum 
unit of the parking lot, including an entrance and an exit. One gate consists of the 
following devices: main camera, auxiliary camera (which can be configured in case of dual 
cameras), VTO, and general screen. The main camera is the core attribute and 
indispensable, so the main camera is a required field. The configuration of other devices 
is not required, such as the auxiliary camera, VTO, and general screen. 
5.8.1 Configure Parking Lots 
Dahua-HTTP-API-For-DSS-V8.7_EN for pt_era_baru_digitama

--- PAGE 538 ---
 
537 
 
After the parking lot is configured, the system will determine and process the passing 
records of bound devices according to the barrier-opening logics.  
[Get the List of Parking Lots] Through [3.11.4.1 Get Parking Resource Tree], you can 
search for the basic information about each parking lot. Check whether the configured 
parking lot has empty parking spots, and whether the blocklist and allowlist are sent, as 
well as the number of positions, entering gates, and exiting gates.  
[Add a Parking Lot] Through [3.11.4.2 Add a Parking Lot], add the information about a 
specified parking lot, and configure the barrier-opening release rules of vehicle groups 
and positions.  
[Update a Parking Lot] Through [3.11.4.3 Update a Parking Lot], modify the information 
about a specified parking lot, and modify the release rules.  
[Batch Delete Parking Lots] Through [3.11.4.4 Batch Delete Parking Lots], delete the 
parking lots. The snapshot requests received by the deleted parking lots will not be 
processed.  
5.8.2 Configure the List of Vehicles 
A vehicle can be added on the platform. When the platform recognizes its license plate, 
the platform can automatically match the information about persons and vehicle groups 
that are bound with the vehicle.  
[Get the List of Vehicles] Through [3.11.2.3 Get the List of Vehicles in Pages], search for 
the information about persons and groups that are bound with a specified vehicle.  
[Update Vehicle Information] Through the interface [3.11.2.1 Batch Save Vehicle 
Information], add or modify the vehicle information.  
[Batch Delete Vehicles] Through [3.11.2.2 Delete Vehicle Information], delete the vehicle 
information by vehicle Ids from the platform. 
5.8.3 Configure Vehicle Groups 
Add vehicles to a specified vehicle group, and bind the group with position release rules. 
Also, batch send the blocklist and allowlist through the vehicle group.  
[Get the List of Entrance and Exit Groups of Vehicles] Through [3.11.1.4 Get the List of 
Entrance and Exit Groups of Vehicles], search for the basic information about group color 
and vehicles.  
[Add a Vehicle Entrance and Exit Group] Through [3.11.1.1 Add a Vehicle Entrance and 
Exit Group], add a group, and bind the parking lot position with group rules. The added 
rules will be synchronized to the parking lot.  
[Update a Vehicle Entrance and Exit Group] Through [3.11.1.2 Update a Vehicle 
Entrance and Exit Group], modify the basic information about a group, as well as the 
binding of the parking lot position with the group. The modified rules will be 
synchronized to the parking lot.  
[Batch Delete Vehicle Entrance and Exit Groups] Through [3.11.1.3 Delete a Vehicle 
Entrance and Exit Group], delete a group. The deleted rules will be synchronized to the 
parking lot. 
5.8.4 Configure Reserved Parking Space Group 
Dahua-HTTP-API-For-DSS-V8.7_EN for pt_era_baru_digitama

--- PAGE 539 ---
 
538 
 
Through the vehicle group or vehicle two ways to add, configure the exclusive parking 
space group bound parking lot parking space, can be configured to alert the parking 
space occupancy. Generally used for special parking spaces (such as private parking 
spaces that have been sold), parking non-special vehicles, remind the administrator to 
proceed to the next step. 
5.8.5 Configure Available Parking Space 
By adding vehicle groups or personnel, available parking spaces are configured, and the 
passage of personnel and vehicles can be limited by the number of available parking 
spaces. Generally, it is used in combination with the rules of card swiping and release to 
check the number of parking spaces parked under personnel or vehicle groups. 
5.8.6 License Plate Recognition 
[Step 1] The device (ITC/NVR) is bound with a parking lot, takes snapshot images, and 
reports them to the platform.  
[Step 2] The platform receives the snapshot information, and analyzes according to the 
configured parking lot rules.  
[Step 3] If a vehicle has the access permission, the platform notifies the device to open 
the barrier automatically.  
[Step 4] MQ (ipms.entrance.notifyVehicleCaptureInfo) notifies the client of the vehicle 
entry.  
[Step 5] Save the data of snapshot, entry and exit, as well as empty parking spots.  
 
5.8.7 Remote Opening 
When a vehicle without the access permission shall be released, the barrier can be 
opened remotely, manually, or through VTO calls. The specific procedure is as follows: 
[Step 1] Call the command [3.11.4.6 Remote Opening] to open the barrier.  
[Step 2] The platform sends a barrier-opening command to the device.  
Dahua-HTTP-API-For-DSS-V8.7_EN for pt_era_baru_digitama

--- PAGE 540 ---
 
539 
 
[Step 3] The device returns the barrier-opening result to the platform synchronously.  
[Step 4] Through MQ (ipms.entrance.openSluice), the platform notifies the client of the 
barrier-opening result.  
[Step 5] Save the data of snapshot, entry and exit, as well as empty parking spots.  
 
5.8.8 Information Search 
1. After the device bound with the parking lot reports the license plate number, the 
platform will record the snapshot information. The snapshot information can be 
queried in the snapshot records of information search.  
2. After logic processing of the snapshot information, the platform determines 
whether it enters or leaves the parking lot. If the vehicle has the access 
permission, an entry record will be created in the entry records, and the status is 
"Not Exited".  
3. When the snapshot information is determined to be exiting, search for the latest 
"Not Exited" record of the vehicle with the same license plate number, update the 
entry record to be "Exited" (no update is performed if the matching record is not 
found), and generate an exit record.  
4. If an error occurs during exit recognition, one entry record is not matched for a 
long time, but actually the vehicle is not in the parking lot already. Call the forced 
exiting interface to update this record to be exited, and generate a record in the 
forced exiting table.

5.9 Face Recognition 
 
The main functions of the face recognition module include: Face comparison group 
(adding, editing and deletion), Face database arming, face search and face snapshot 
message reporting. 
5.9.1 Face Comparison Group 
On the platform, you can add, edit and delete face comparison groups, add person 
information to the face comparison group, arm and issue face comparison groups to the 
face device. You can create up to 50 face comparison groups and add 50,000 persons to a 
single face comparison group. The main face devices include IVSS, IPC and NVR. 
Add Face Comparison group 
Select [3.12.1.1 Add a Face Comparison Group], and then call the interface to add a new 
face comparison group: 
 
Modify Face Comparison Group 
Dahua-HTTP-API-For-DSS-V8.7_EN for pt_era_baru_digitama

--- PAGE 543 ---
 
542 
 
Select [3.12.1.2 Update a Face Comparison Group], and then call the interface to edit the 
face comparison group: 
 
Delete Face Comparison Group 
Select [3.12.1.3 Delete a Face Comparison Group], and then call the interface to delete the 
face comparison group: 
 
5.9.2 Face Database Arming 
On the platform, you can arm the persons added to the face comparison group to the 
specified face device, or disarm them from the specified face device. The platform allows 
the maximum 10 million of face records to be distributed, mainly including face 
distribution, face deletion, channel distribution and channel withdrawal. 
Face distribution 
Dahua-HTTP-API-For-DSS-V8.7_EN for pt_era_baru_digitama

information on a face device:

5.9.3 Face search 
On the platform, you can search the historical information of face snapshots based on 
conditions (search by face feature in the platform DB, and search by image on the device), 
and search for the historical information of face recognition by face feature and face 
image (search by face feature in the platform DB). 
Face Snapshot Record Search 
Select [3.12.2.1 Starting Search the Face Snapshot Records Asynchronously by Searching 
by Image], and then call the interface to get face snapshot or recognition records, and the 
interface returns session for the search of the next interface. Based on the session 
returned by the first interface, select [3.12.2.3 Search the Face Snapshot Records in Pages 
by Searching by Image], and then call the interface to get face snapshot or recognition 
records. 
Dahua-HTTP-API-For-DSS-V8.7_EN for pt_era_baru_digitama

--- PAGE 546 ---
 
545 
 
Select [3.12.2.5 Search the Face Snapshot Records in Pages Based on Features], and then 
call the interface to get face snapshot records based on the feature values. 
Face Recognition Record Search 
Select [3.12.2.6 Search the Face Recognition Records in Pages Based on Features], and 
then call the interface to get face recognition records. 
Face Snapshot Message Reporting 
The face snapshot function module means that the camera channel of the device reports 
the captured face information to the platform, which then parses, processes and displays 
the event. 
The platform parses and processes the information by receiving MQ messages in [4.7.2 
Notification of Face Snapshot/Recognition Messages], and then notifies the alarm module 
and client.

5.10 Alarm Messages 
 
The platform supports two methods to send external alarms: 
• Call the alarm port, and then push the alarm through the callback URL. 
• Connect with the MQ, subscribe to the alarm topic, and then receive real-time 
alarm messages. 
Dahua-HTTP-API-For-DSS-V8.7_EN for pt_era_baru_digitama

--- PAGE 548 ---
 
547 
 
If you only connect to real-time alarms, the first method is recommended, because it is 
simpler. If you need to connect to other real-time information, such as real-time card 
swiping records and passed vehicle records, the second method is recommended, 
because its functions are more complete. Only alarm messages support the interface 
callback method now. 
5.10.1 Interface Subscription 
After completing login authentication, call the alarm port. See [3.6.1 Subscribe to Alarms]. 
That is, the specified logged in user subscribes to alarm messages from the platform. 
When the platform client configures the alarm scheme, a linked user is designated. If the 
linked user has subscribed to the alarm, when reporting the specified type of alarm, the 
callback interface provided during subscription is called to push an alarm message. 
Notes: 
1. The linked user of the alarm scheme must match the user who has subscribed to 
the alarm to receive alarms. 
2. The URL and return value of the callback interface can be customized, while the 
interface must be a standard REST interface. The request method and input 
parameters must be in the specified formats. 
3. The signature field of the input parameter is optional. The requester can freely 
define a string of no more than 255 characters, which is used for matching during 
callback to make a simple verification. You can repeatedly call the interface and 
modify the signature field to update the signature. 
4. Subscription and unsubscription use the same interface and are distinguished by 
the action field. 
5.10.2 MQ Subscription 
Get MQ Address 
Receive alarm messages from the platform through MQ. See [4 MQ Notification Message] 
to obtain the MQ address. 
Alarm Subscription 
The client gets alarm messages by subscribing to the Topic. The format of the alarm topic 
is as follows: mq.alarm.msg.topic.{UserID}. UserId is user ID, which is returned in the 
second login. If the user ID of the system is 1, after the system user logs in to the 
platform, the subscribed topic is: mq.alarm.msg.topic.1. See [6.3.2 MQ Connection 
Examples] for subscription connection. 
5.10.3 Search for Alarm 
Real-time Alarm Message 
Dahua-HTTP-API-For-DSS-V8.7_EN for pt_era_baru_digitama

--- PAGE 549 ---
 
548 
 
After the platform receives the alarm, if the alarm in the alarm scheme is configured with 
a linked user, the alarm will be sent to the corresponding online user. See [4.2.1 Alarm 
Messages] for alarm messages. Subscription by user group is also supported. 
Historical Alarm Query 
Search for alarm records in pages. Some alarm messages might carry images. If there is 
no image or you need to view the alarm details, you need to call the details viewing 
interface, which varies with the alarm type. 
Process Alarm 
Process alarm information and record processing comments. 
5.10.4 The Connection Procedure for Typical Applications: Receive 
an Alarm 
1. Add a device that can trigger an alarm from [Basic Config>Device>Add Device] on the 
VMS client. 
 
2. Configure an alarm scheme  from [Applications Config>Event] on the VMS client and 
set alarm type, alarm source, linkage rules, and intended users. 
 
3. Start API connection. Firstly, perform login authentication, including first login, second 
login, heartbeat keepalive, and token update. For details, refer t o [ 5.1 Login 
Authentication] or [6.3.1.1 Example of Login Authentication with Java] on Demo.  
All subsequent API invocations need to carry the token field returned during logi ning in 
the X-Subject-Token request header. 
 
4. Alarms can be received by either ActiveMQ monitoring or subscription callback. Only the 
subscription callback method with lower connection difficulty is described here. For details, 
refer to [5.10 Alarm Messages]. 
 
5. Subscribe to alarms from API document through [3.6.1 Subscribe to Alarms].  
Focus on all parameters: 
{ 
    "callbackUrl": "https: //192.168.1.1:443/brms/api/v1.1/push-data/alarm/push", 
    "action": "1",  
    "signature": "c743b433407be68ee62c46ede8fb5a0c"  
} 
Wherein,  
callbackUrl: Indicates a third -party custom alarm receiving API, which must be defined in 
the specified callback format.  
action: Indicates a subscription or unsubscription action. The token c arried in this API is 
only effective for the subscriber. A repeated subscription a ction will overwrite the last 
subscription. Note: The subscriber must be the notified subscriber s pecified in the alarm 
scheme.  
Dahua-HTTP-API-For-DSS-V8.7_EN for pt_era_baru_digitama

--- PAGE 550 ---
 
549 
 
signature: Indicates a random string. If this field is not null, the platform will carry this string 
while calling back an alarm. The subscriber will accept this alarm only when the  signature 
is valid. 
 
6. A device triggers an alarm and sends it to the VMS platform. The VMS platform pushes 
the alarm to the VMS client while invoking the specified subscription callback API according 
to the notified subscriber specified in the alarm scheme, pushing key information including 
alarm time, alarm source, and alarm type to a third party platform.

6.1.5 Encoding Channel Capability Set 
Decimal is converted to 32-bit binary, each bit representing a set of capabilities: 0 = no, 1 
= yes. According to the enumeration value description, from right to left, the value of 
each bit is determined by determining whether it is 1 to confirm whether there is a 
corresponding capability set. For example, the capability set returned by the interface to a 
certain channel is 9, and the conversion to binary is 1001, that is to say, starting from the 
right, the first and fourth bits have capability sets, corresponding to "Intelligent Alarm" 
and "IR Temperature Analysis" respectively.

6.2 Common Error Codes 
6.2.1 HTTP Status Codes 
Error code Error explanation 
400 Bad request, please check whether the request information is correct. 
401 
Authentication failed. The possible cause is that no token authentication information is 
carried or the token has become invalid. After successful login, a token is returned. This 
returned token shall be carried in subsequent requests. Also, the token has a valid time. 
It needs a keep-alive within 30 seconds, and an update within 30 minutes. 
403 The request URL is illegal. Please check the correctness of the URL. 
415 
The Content-type type is incorrect. The input parameters of our most POST/PUT 
interfaces are in standard JSON format. The request header of Content-type must be set 
as application/json. 
429 The single business request is too frequent. Please reduce the request frequency and try 
again later. 
503 The server is busy, please pause your request and try again later. 
6.2.2 Business Error Codes 
Error code Error explanation 
1001 Internal server error. Check the parameters or contact the maintenance personnel to 
view the log for problem analysis. 
1004 Invalid request parameter. It may be that a required parameter is missing or the 
parameter value format is incorrect. 
1005 The name already exists. Modify the name and try again. 
1006 The maximum number limit is exceeded. The limit varies with the function module. 
1007 The operation data does not exist. It is recommended to restart the client and try again. 
1008 The current task is not completed. Do not repeat the operation. Try again later. 
1101 
Login error. The username userName is null or the random value randomKey is invalid. 
Check the login interface parameters. Long interval between two login operations results 
in invalid randomKey. Complete two login operations within 10 seconds. 
1103 The current user does not have operation permission for this channel or device. Contact 
the administrator for authorization. 
1105 Service offline. Try again later, or contact the maintenance personnel to check the 
platform. 
2001 Username or password error. Check and try again. 
2002 The user is locked. Try again later, or contact the administrator to unlock. 
7000 Authentication failed. The token might be null or invalid.

public class LoginExample {

";

    static final String UPDATE_TOKEN_URL = "https://192.168.1.1:443/brms/api/v1.0/a ccounts/updat
eToken"; 
 
    static final String SUCCESS_CODE = "1000";  
    static String SIGNATURE_MD5_TEMP4 = null;  
    static String TOKEN_VALUE = null;  
    static final String TOKEN = "token";  
    static final String POST = "post";  
    static final String PUT = "put";  
    static int HEART_COUNT = 0;

    public static void main(String[] args) throws Exception {

        firstLoginParams.put("userName", "system");  
        firstLoginParams.put("ipAddress", "");

        String aesSecretVector = UUID.ran domUUID().toString().replace("-", "").substring(16);

PublicKey(aesSecretKey, Base64.getDecoder().decode(platformPublicKeyWi thBase64))); 
        String encryptedAes SecretVectorWithBase64 = Base64.getEncoder().encodeToString(encrypt
ByPublicKey(aesSecretVector, Base64.getDecoder().decode(platformPu blicKeyWithBase64)));

        TOKEN_VALUE = secondResponse.getString(TOKEN);

            keepAliveParamMap.put("token", TOKEN_VALUE);  
            JSONObject heartResponse = JSONObject.parseObject(sendPostOrPut(KEEP_ALIVE_U RL,
 keepAliveParamMap, PUT));  
            if (SUCCESS_CODE.equals(heartResponse.getString("code"))) {  
                System.out.println("Heart success.");  
            } 
            HEART_COUNT++; 
            //Update the token per 2 0 minutes. 
            if (HEART_COUNT % 60 == 0) {  
                //Restore the heartCount to zero.  
                HEART_COUNT = 0;  
                Map<String, Object> updateTokenParamMap = new HashMap<>();  
                JSONObject udpateTokenResponse = JSONObject.parseObject(sendPostOrPut( UPD

ng(TOKEN); 
                    System.out.println(String.format("Update token success. New token: %s", new
TokenValue)); 
                    TOKEN_VALUE = newTokenValue;  
                } 
            } 
        } 
 
        //Login is over, do your own things with the token...  
    } 
 
    /** 
     * Send post or put request method with HTTP.  
     * @param url url  
     * @param params params  
     * @param requestMode POST or PUT or GET or DELETE  
     * @return {@link String }  
     * @throws IOException ioexception  
     */ 
    static String sendPostOrPut(String url, Map<String, Object> params, String requ estMode) thro
ws IOException {  
        if (!requestMode.equals(POST) && !requestMode.equals(PUT)) {  
            return null;  
        } 
        // Create a trust manager that does not validate certificate chains  
        TrustManager[] trustAllCerts = new TrustManager[] {  
            new X509TrustManager() {  
                @Override 
                public X509Certificate[] getAcceptedIssuers() {  
Dahua-HTTP-API-For-DSS-V8.7_EN for pt_era_baru_digitama

--- PAGE 572 ---
 
571 
 
                    return new X509Certificate[0];  
                } 
                @Override 
                public void checkClientTrusted(X509Certificate[] certs, String authType) {  
                } 
                @Override 
                public void checkServerTrusted(X509Certificate[] certs, String authType) {  
                } 
            } 
        }; 
        // Install the all -trusting trust manager  
        try {  
            SSLContext sslContext = SSLContext.getInstance("SSL");  
            sslContext.init(null, trustAllCerts, new SecureRandom());  
            // Create an ssl socket factory with our all -trusting manager  
            SSLConnectionSocketFactory sslSocketFactory = new SSLConnectionSocketFactory(sslC
ontext, (hostname, session) -> true);  
 
            // Create a custom HttpClient with the SSL socket factory  
            CloseableHttpClient httpClient = HttpClients.custom()  
                    .setSSLSocketFactory(sslSocketFactory) 
                    .build(); 
            HttpEntityEnclosingRequestBase httpRequest = null;  
            if (requestMode.equals(POST)) {  
                httpRequest = new HttpPost(url);  
            } else if (requestMode.equals(PUT)) {  
                httpRequest = new HttpPut(url);  
            } 
            StringEntity entity = new StringEntity(JSON.toJSONString(params), "UTF -8"); 
            httpRequest.setEntity(entity); 
            httpRequest.setHeader("Content-Type", "application/json;charset=UTF -8"); 
            httpRequest.setHeader("X-Subject-Token", TOKEN_VALUE);  
 
            CloseableHttpResponse response = httpClient.execute(httpRequest);  
            HttpEntity responseEntity = response.getEntity();  
            //In order to avoid messy code,encode the response data in UTF -8. 
            String reply = EntityUtils.toString(responseEntity, "UTF -8"); 
            //Release resources finally.  
            if (httpClient != null) {  
                httpClient.close(); 
            } 
            if (response != null) {  
                response.close(); 
            } 
            return reply;  
        } catch (NoSuchAlgorithmException | KeyManagementException e) {  
            throw new RuntimeException(e);  
        } 
    } 
 
    /** 
     * Generate signature with MD5 -transformation five times.  
     * @param userName  login usern ame 
     * @param password  login password  
     * @param realm     the 'realm' returned from the first login  
     * @param randomKey the 'randomKey' returned from the first login  
     * @return signature  
Dahua-HTTP-API-For-DSS-V8.7_EN for pt_era_baru_digitama

--- PAGE 573 ---
 
572 
 
     */ 
    static String generateSignature(String userName, String password, String real m, String rando
mKey) {  
        String temp1 = DigestUtils.md5Hex(password);  
        String temp2 = DigestUtils.md5Hex(userName + temp1);  
        String temp3 = DigestUtils.md5 Hex(temp2); 
        String temp4 = DigestUtils.md5Hex(userName + ":" + realm + ":" + temp3);  
        //Retain the temp4, in order to calculate a signature for update token later.  
        SIGNATURE_MD5_TEMP4 = temp4;  
        String signature = DigestUtils.m d5Hex(temp4 + ":" + randomKey);  
        return signature;  
    } 
 
    /** 
     * RSA encryption. Public key encryption, private key decryption  
     * @param text data  
     * @param publicKeyBytes public key string array  
     * @return string after encryptio n 
     * @throws Exception  
     */ 
    static byte[] encryptByPublicKey(String text, byte[] publicKeyBytes) thr ows Exception {  
        byte[] result = null;  
        int rsaBytesLenEncrypt = 245;  
 
        //Get public key object  
        X509EncodedKeySpec x509KeySpec = new X509EncodedKeySpec(publicKeyBytes);  
        KeyFactory keyFactory = KeyFactory.getInstance("RSA");  
        Key publicKeyObject = keyFactory.generatePublic(x509KeySpec);  
 
        //Encrypt data  
        byte[] dataBytes = text.getBytes(StandardCharsets.UTF_8);  
        Cipher cipher = Cipher.getInstance(keyFactory.getAlgorithm());  
        cipher.init(Cipher.ENCRYPT_MODE, publicKeyObject);  
        for (int i = 0; i < dataBytes.length; i += rsaBytesL enEncrypt) {  
            int to = Math.min(i + rsaBytesLenEncrypt, dataBytes.length);  
            byte[] temp = cipher.doFinal(Arrays.copyOfRange(dataBytes, i, to));  
            result = sumBytes(result, temp);  
        } 
        return result;  
    } 
 
    /** 
     * Sum 2 bytes  
     * @param bytes1 byte 1  
     * @param bytes2 byte 2  
     * @return the new array formed by merging two arrays  
     */ 
    static byte[] sumBytes(byte[] bytes1, byte[] bytes2) {  
        byte[] result = null;  
        int len1 = 0;  
        int len2 = 0;  
        if (null != bytes1) {  
            len1 = bytes1.length;  
        } 
        if (null != bytes2) {  
            len2 = bytes2.length;  
        } 
Dahua-HTTP-API-For-DSS-V8.7_EN for pt_era_baru_digitama

--- PAGE 574 ---
 
573 
 
        if (len1 + len2 > 0) {  
            result = new byte[len1 + len2];  
        } 
        if (len1 > 0) {  
            System.arraycopy(bytes1, 0, result, 0, len1);  
        } 
        if (len2 > 0) {  
            System.arraycopy(bytes2, 0, result, len1, len2);  
        } 
        return result;  
    } 
}

    /** 
     * Obtain 8 random digits  
     * @param count  
     * @return  
     */ 
    public static String randomNumber(int count) {  
        Random random = new Random();  
        StringBuilder val = new StringBuilder();  
        for(int i = 0; i < count; ++i) {  
            val.append(random.nextInt(10)); 
        } 
        return val.toSt ring(); 
    } 
 
    /** 
     * Send post or get request method with HTTP.  
     * @param url url  
     * @param params params  
     * @param requestMode POST or GET  
     * @return reply  
     */ 
    static String sendPostOrGet(String url, Map<String, Object> pa rams, String requestMode) thr
ows IOException {  
        String realUrl = URL_PREFIX + url;  
        if (!requestMode.equals(POST) && !requestMode.equals(GET)) {  
            return null;  
        } 
        // Create a trust manager that does not validate certificate chains  
        TrustManager[] trustAllCerts = new TrustManager[]{  
                new X509TrustManager() {  
                    @Override 
                    public X509Certificate[] getAc ceptedIssuers() {  
                        return new X509Certificate[0];  
                    } 
                    @Override 
                    public void checkClientTrusted(X509Certificate[] certs, String authType) {  
                    } 
                    @Override 
                    public void checkServerTrusted(X509Certificate[] certs, String authType) {  
                    } 
                } 
        }; 
        // Install the all -trusting trust manager  
        try {  
            SSLContext sslContext = SSLContext.getInstance("SSL");  
            sslContext.init(null, trustAllCerts, new SecureRandom());  
Dahua-HTTP-API-For-DSS-V8.7_EN for pt_era_baru_digitama

--- PAGE 580 ---
 
579 
 
            // Create an ssl socket factory with our all -trusting manager  
            SSLConnectionSocketFactory sslSocketFactory = new SSLConnection SocketFactory(sslC
ontext, (hostname, session) -> true);  
 
            // Create a custom HttpClient with the SSL socket factory  
            CloseableHttpClient httpClient = HttpClients.custom()  
                    .setSSLSocketFactory(sslSocketFactory) 
                    .build(); 
            CloseableHttpResponse httpResponse = null;  
            if (requestMode.equals(POST)) {  
                HttpEntityEnclosingRequestBase httpRequest = new Htt pPost(realUrl); 
                StringEntity entity = new StringEntity(JSON.toJSONString(params), "UTF -8"); 
                httpRequest.setEntity(entity); 
                httpRequest.setHeader("Content-Type", "application/json;charset=UTF -8"); 
                httpRequest.setHeader("X-Subject-Token", TOKEN_VALUE);  
                httpResponse = httpClient.execute(httpRequest);  
            } else if (requestMode.equals(GET)) {  
                HttpGet httpGet = new HttpGet(realUrl);  
                httpGet.setHeader("X-Subject-Token", TOKEN_VALUE);  
                httpGet.setHeader("Content-Type", "application/json;charset=UTF -8"); 
                httpResponse = httpClient.execute(httpGet);  
            } 
            HttpEntity responseEntity = httpResponse.getE ntity(); 
            //In order to avoid messy code,encode the response data in UTF -8. 
            String reply = EntityUtils.toString(responseEntity, "UTF -8"); 
            if (!reply.contains("1000")) {  
                System.out.println("Request \"" + ur l + " \" failed, response: " + reply);  
            } 
            //Release resources finally.  
            if (httpClient != null) {  
                httpClient.close(); 
            } 
            if (httpResponse != null) {  
                httpResponse.close(); 
            } 
            return reply;  
        }catch (NoSuchAlgorithmException | KeyManagementException e) {  
            throw new RuntimeException(e);  
        } 
    } 
 
    /** 
     * AES encryption  
     * @param password  
     * @return  
     */ 
    static String encryptPassWordWithAES(String password){  
        //This three params you can obtain from the LoginExample or your client.  
        try {  
            return encryptWithAES 7(password,SECRET_KEY,SECRET_VECTOR); 
        } catch (Exception e) {  
            e.printStackTrace(); 
        } 
        return null;  
    } 
 
    /** 
Dahua-HTTP-API-For-DSS-V8.7_EN for pt_era_baru_digitama

--- PAGE 581 ---
 
580 
 
     * AES encryption mode is CBC, and the filling mode is pkcs7padding  
     * @param text  
     * @param aesKey  
     * @param aesVector  
     * @return  
     * @throws Exception  
     */ 
    static String encryptWithAES7(String text, String aesKey, String aesVector) throw s Exception {  
        SecretKey keySpec = new SecretKeySpec(aesKey.getBytes("U TF-8"), "AES");  
        //If your program run with an exception :"Cannot find any provider supporting AES/CBC
/PKCS7Padding",you can replace "PKCS7Padding" with "PKCS5Padding".  
        Cipher cipher = Cipher.getInstance("AES/CBC/PKCS5Padding");  
        IvParameterSpec iv = new IvParameterSpec(aesVector.getBytes("UTF -8")); 
        cipher.init(Cipher.ENCRYPT_MODE, keySpec, iv);  
        byte[] encrypted = cipher.doFinal(text.getBytes("UTF -8")); 
        return parseByte2HexStr(encrypted);  
    } 
 
    /** 
     * I mage to base64  
     * @param imagePath  
     * @return  
     */ 
    public static String imageToBase64(String imagePath) {  
        String base64Image = "";  
        try {  
            byte[] imageBytes = Files.readAllBytes(new File(imagePath).toPath());  
            base64Image = org.apache.commons.codec.binary.Base64.encodeBase64String(im ageBy
tes); 
        } catch (IOException e) {  
            e.printStackTrace(); 
        } 
        return base64Image;  
    } 
 
    /** 
     * Byte array to 16 bit string  
     * @param buf  
     * @return  
     */ 
    static String parseByte2HexStr(byte buf[]) {  
        StringBuffer sb = new StringBuffer();  
        for (int i = 0; i < buf.length; i++) {  
            String hex = Integer.toHex String(buf[i] & 0xFF);  
            if (hex.length() == 1) {  
                hex = '0' + hex;  
            } 
            sb.append(hex.toLowerCase()); 
        } 
        return sb.toString();  
    } 
 
    /** 
     * Deserialize data  
     * @param responseString  
     * @param clazz  
     * @param fieldName  
Dahua-HTTP-API-For-DSS-V8.7_EN for pt_era_baru_digitama

--- PAGE 582 ---
 
581 
 
     * @param businessName  
     * @param <T>  
     * @return  
     * @throws Exception  
     */ 
    static <T> List<T> deserializeData(String responseString, Class<T> clazz,Str ing fieldName,Strin
g businessName) throws Exception {  
        JSONObject jsonObject=JSONObject.parseObject(responseString);  
        Integer code = (Integer) jsonObject.get("cod e"); 
        if(code.compareTo(SUCCESS_CODE) == 0){  
            Object dataObject = jsonObject.getJSONObject("data").get(fieldName);  
            if (dataObject != null) {  
                List<T> resultList=JSONObject.parseArray(dataObject.toString(), clazz ); 
                if (resultList == null || resultList.size() == 0) {  
                    throw new Exception("If you want to add a " + businessName + ", please 
add it in client first.");  
                } 
                return JSONObject.parseArray(data Object.toString(), clazz);  
            } 
        } else if (code.compareTo(RETURN_CODE_DATA_NOT_EXIST) == 0){  
            throw new Exception("If you want to add a " + businessName + ", please add it in
 client first.");  
        } else {  
            throw new Exception(responseString);  
        } 
        return null;  
    }

6.3.1.3 Example of Login Authentication with JS 
Description 
Import the plug-ins of axios and crypto-js/md5. 
Install NodeJS first and install the plug-ins with npm command. 
npm install axios crypto -js/md5 
Or import the plug-ins with the <script> tag. 
<script src="https://unpkg.com/axios/dist/axios.min.js"></script>  
<script type="text/javascript" src="path-to/bower_components/crypto-js/crypto-js.js"></script> 
Only partial functions of the plug-ins are mentioned in the text. For more functions and 
details, go to the websites: 
axios.js - official document 
npm/crypto-js 
npm/uuid 
Example Code 
Run the codes in ES6 environment. Use Chrome 76 and later versions or use front-end 
packaging tools such as webpack to assist running. 
const axios = require('axios');  
const CryptoJS = require('crypto -js'); 
const { v4: uuidv4 } = require('uuid');  
const crypto = require('crypto');  
const https = require('https'); 
const AUTH_URL = "https://192.168.1.1:443/brms/api/v1.0/accounts/authorize";  
const KEEP_ALIVE_URL = "https://192.168.1.1:443/brms/api/v1.0/accounts/keepalive";  
const UPDATE_TOKEN_URL = "https://192.168.1.1:443/brms/api/v1.0/accounts/updat eToken"; 
const SUCCESS_CODE = 1000;

let SIGNATURE_MD5_TEMP4 = null;  
let TOKEN_VALUE = null;  
let HEART_COUNT = 0;  
 
async function main() {  
    try {  
        //Step1: Try to login first time.  
        const firstLoginParams = {  
            userName: "system" , 
            ipAddress: "",  
            clientType: "WINPC_V2"  
        }; 
        const firstResponse = await sendPostOrPut(AUTH_URL, firstLoginParams,  'POST');  
        const firstLoginResponse = firstResponse.data;  
 
        if (!firstLoginResponse || !fi rstLoginResponse.realm) {  
            console.error("First login failed or response is invalid:", firstLoginRespons e); 
            return; 
        } 
 
        //Step2: Try to login second time.  
        const userName = "system";  
        const passWord = "admin1234567";  
        const realm = firstLoginResponse.realm;  
        const randomKey = firstLoginResponse.randomKey;  
        const platformPublicKeyWithBase64 = firstLoginResponse.publickey;  
        const signature = generateSignature(userName, passWord, realm, randomKey);  
 
        //Generate the AES secret key and AES secret vector, encrypted by RSA public k ey. 
        const aesSecretKey = uuidv4().replace(/ -/g, "");  
        const aesSecretVect or = uuidv4().replace(/ -/g, "").substring(16);  
        const encryptedAesSecretKeyWithBase64 = encryptByPublicKey(aesSecr etKey, platformPubli
cKeyWithBase64); 
        const encryptedAesSecretVectorWithBase64 = encryptByPublicKey(aesSecr etVector, platfor
mPublicKeyWithBase64); 
 
        const secondLoginParams = {  
            mac: "2C:F0:5D:4D:5E:DB",  
            signature, 
            userName, 
            randomKey, 
            publicKey: "",  
            encrytType: "MD5",  
            ipAddress: "",  
            clientType: "WINPC_V2",  
            userType: "0",  
            secretKey: encrypted.......yWithBase64,  
            secretVector: encryptedAe.......torWithBase64  
        }; 
        const secondResponse = await sendPostOrPut(AUTH_URL, secondLoginParams, 'P OST'); 
        const secondResponseData = secondResponse.data;  
        TOKEN_VALUE = secondResponseData.token;

/** 
 *  Send a POST or PUT request.  
 * @param url  
 * @param params  
 * @param requestMode  
 * @returns {Promise<*|null>}  
 */ 
async function sendPostOrPut(url, params, requestMode) {  
    if (requestMode !== 'POST' && requestMode !== 'PUT') {  
        return null;  
    } 
    try {  
        const config = {  
            headers: {  
                'Content-Type': 'application/json;charset=UTF -8', 
                'X-Subject-Token': TOKEN_VALUE  
            }, 
            data: JSON.stringify(params),  
            httpsAgent: new https.Agent({  
                rejectUnauthorized: false  
            }) 
        }; 
Dahua-HTTP-API-For-DSS-V8.7_EN for pt_era_baru_digitama

--- PAGE 590 ---
 
589 
 
        return await axios[requestMode.toLowerCase()](url, config.data, config);  
    } catch (error) {  
        if (error.status === 401) {  
            return error.response;  
        } 
 
        throw new Error( `HTTP request failed: ${error.message}`);  
    } 
} 
 
/** 
 * Generate the signature.  
 * @param userName  
 * @param password  
 * @param realm  
 * @param randomKey  
 * @returns {*}  
 */ 
function generateSignature(userName, password, realm, randomKey) {  
    const temp1 = CryptoJS.MD5(password).toString();  
    const temp2 = CryptoJS.MD5(userName + temp1).toString();  
    const temp3 = CryptoJS.MD5(temp2).toString();  
    const temp4 = CryptoJS.MD5(userName + ':' + realm + ':' + temp3).toString();  
    // Reta in the temp4, in order to calculate a signature for update token later.  
    SIGNATURE_MD5_TEMP4 = temp4;  
    return CryptoJS.MD5(temp4 + ':' + randomKey).toString();  
} 
 
/** 
 * Encrypt the text by public key.  
 * @param text  
 * @param publicKeyBase64  
 * @ret urns {string}  
 */ 
function encryptByPublicKey(text, publicKeyBase64) {  
    try {  
        // Convert public key from base64 to PEM format  
        const publicKeyPem = ` -----BEGIN PUBLIC KEY -----\n${publicKeyBase64}\n-----END PUBLI
C KEY -----`; 
 
        // En crypt the data using PKCS1_v1_5 padding  
        const encryptedData = crypto.publicEncrypt({  
            key: publicKeyPem,  
            padding: crypto.constants.RSA_PKCS1_PADDING  
        }, Buffer.from(text));  
 
        // Convert the encrypted data to base64  
        const encryptedDataBase64 = encryptedData.toString('base64');  
 
        return encryptedDataBase64;  
    } catch (error) {  
        console.error('Encryption failed:', error);  
        throw new Error(`En cryption failed: ${error.message}`);  
    } 
} 
 
main();

        /** 
         * Send post or put request method with HTTP.  
         * @param url  
         * @param params  
         * @return reply  
         */ 
        public static string? SendP ostOrPut(string url, Dictionary<string, object> param, string re
questMode) 
        { 
            if (!requestMode.Equals(POST) && !requestMode.Equals(PUT))  
            { 
                return null;  
            } 
            
            HttpRequestMessage httpRequestMessage = new(HttpMethod.Post, url);  
 
            if (requestMode.Equals(PUT))  
            { 
                httpRequestMessage = new HttpRequestMessage(HttpMethod.Put, url);  
            } 
            StringContent stringContent = new(JsonSerializer.Serialize(param), Encoding.UTF 8, "ap
plication/json"); 
 
            httpRequestMessage.Content = str ingContent; 
            httpRequestMessage.Headers.Add("X-Subject-Token", TOKEN_VALUE);  
 
            return SendAsync(httpRequestMessage).Result;  
        } 
 
        /** 
         * Sending http requests asynchronously.  
         * @param httpRequestMessage  
         * @return response  
Dahua-HTTP-API-For-DSS-V8.7_EN for pt_era_baru_digitama

--- PAGE 594 ---
 
593 
 
         */ 
        public static async Task<string> SendAsync(HttpRequestMessage httpRequest Message) 
        { 
             // Create a custom HttpClientHandler and ignore certificate validation  
            HttpClientHandler han dler = new HttpClientHandler  
            { 
                ServerCertificateCustomValidationCallback = (message, cert, chain, sslPolicyErr ors) 
=> true  
            }; 
            HttpClient httpClient = new HttpClient(handler);  
            HttpResponseMessage response = await httpClient.SendAsync(httpRequestMessage);  
 
            //In order to avoid messy code,encode the response data in UTF -8. 
            string reply = await response.Content.ReadAsStringAsync();  
            return reply;  
        } 
 
        /** 
         * Generate signature with MD5 -transformation five times.  
         * @param userName  
         * @param password  
         * @para m realm  
         * @param randomKey  
         * @return signature  
         */ 
        public static string GenerateSignature(string userName, string password, st ring? realm, str
ing? randomKey)  
        { 
            string temp1 = Md5Hex(password);  
            string temp2 = Md5Hex(userName + temp1);  
            string temp3 = Md5Hex(temp2);  
            string temp4 = Md5Hex(userName + ":" + realm + ":" + temp3);  
            //Retain the temp4,in order to calculate a signature for update token later.  
            SIGNATURE_MD5_TEMP4 = temp4;  
            String signature = Md5Hex(temp4 + ":" + randomKey);  
            return signature;  
        } 
 
        /** 
         * First MD5 encryption, then convert to hexadecimal string.  
         * @param data  
         * @return  
         */ 
        public static string Md5Hex(string data)  
        { 
            byte[] bytes = Encoding.UTF8.GetBytes(data);  
            byte[] result = MD5.HashData(bytes);  
            var stringBuilder = new S tringBuilder(); 
            for (int i = 0; i < result.Length; i++)  
            { 
                stringBuilder.Append(result[i].ToString("x2")); 
            } 
            return stringBuilder.ToString();  
        } 
 
        /** 
         * RSA public key en cryption. 
Dahua-HTTP-API-For-DSS-V8.7_EN for pt_era_baru_digitama

--- PAGE 595 ---
 
594 
 
         * @param text  
         * @param publicKeyBytes  
         * @return  
         */ 
        public static byte[] EncryptByPublicKey(string text, byte[] publicKeyBytes ) 
        { 
            var publicKey = (RsaKeyParameters)PublicKeyFactory.Cr eateKey(publicKeyBytes); 
            var cipher = CipherUtilities.GetCipher("RSA/NONE/PKCS1Padding");  
            cipher.Init(true, publicKey);  
 
            byte[] dataBytes = Encoding.UTF8.GetBytes(text);  
            int rsaBytesLenEncrypt = 245;  
            List<byte[]> encryptedParts = new List<byte[]>();  
 
            for (int i = 0; i < dataBytes.Length; i += rsaBytesLenEncrypt)  
            { 
                int to = Math.Min(i + rsaBytesLenEncrypt, dataBytes.Length);  
                byte[] temp = cipher.DoFinal(dataBytes, i, to - i); 
                encryptedParts.Add(temp); 
            } 
 
            return encryptedParts.SelectMany(bytes => b ytes).ToArray(); 
        } 
    } 
} 
6.3.1.5 Example of Login Authentication with Python 
Example Code 
import requests  
import json  
import hashlib  
import base64  
import uuid  
import time  
from Crypto.Cipher import AES, PKCS1_v1_5  
from Crypto.PublicKey import RSA  
from Crypto.Util.Padding import pad, unpad  
import urllib3  
 
AUTH_URL = "https://192.168.1.1:443/brms/api/v1.0/accounts/authorize"  
KEEP_ALIVE_URL = "https://192.168.1.1:443/brms/api/v1.0/accounts/keepalive" 
UPDATE_TOKEN_URL = "https://192.168.1.1:443/brms/api/v1.0/accounts/updateToke n" 
SUCCESS_CODE = 1000  
TOKEN = "token"  
POST = "post"  
PUT = "put"  
HEART_COUNT = 0  
SIGNATURE_MD5_TEMP4 = None  
TOKEN_VALUE = None  
 
""" 
Send a POST or PUT request.  
 
Dahua-HTTP-API-For-DSS-V8.7_EN for pt_era_baru_digitama

--- PAGE 596 ---
 
595 
 
This function sends an HTTP request to the specified URL with the given parameters and  reques
t mode (POST or PUT),  
including necessary headers, and returns the response.  
 
Parameters: 
- url (str): The target URL for the request.  
- params (dict): The parameters for the request, which will be sent as JSON.  
- request_mode (str): The request mode, supporting "POST" or "PUT".  
 
Returns: 
- str: The response text from the request.  
""" 
def send_post_or_put(url, params, request _mode): 
    if params is None:  
        params = {}  
    # Disable SSL verification and suppress InsecureRequestWarning  
    urllib3.disable_warnings(urllib3.exceptions.InsecureRequestWarning) 
    headers = {  
        "Content-Type": "application/json;charset=UTF -8", 
        "X-Subject-Token": TOKEN_VALUE  
    } 
    response = requests.request(request_mode, url, headers=header s, data=json.dumps(params), v
erify=False) 
    return response.text  
 
""" 
Generate a signature for user authentication.  
 
This function creates an MD5 signature based on the provided username, password, re alm, and 
random key.  
The process involves multiple hashing steps to ensure the security and integrity of the gene rate
d signature.  
 
Parameters: 
- username (str): The username of the user.  
- password (str): The password of the user.  
- realm (str): The authentication realm.  
- random_key (str): A random key used  in the signature generation.  
 
Returns: 
- str: The generated MD5 signature.  
""" 
def generate_signature(username, password, realm, random_key):  
    temp1 = hashlib.md5(password.encode()).hexdigest()  
    temp2 = hashlib.md5((username + temp1).encode()).hexdi gest() 
    temp3 = hashlib.md5(temp2.encode()).hexdigest()  
    temp4 = hashlib.md5((username + ":" + realm + ":" + temp3).encode()).hexdiges t() 
    global SIGNATURE_MD5_TEMP4  
    SIGNATURE_MD5_TEMP4 = temp4  
    signature = hashlib.md5((temp4 + ":" + random_key).encode()).hexdigest()  
    return signature  
 
""" 
    Encrypts the given text using the provided public key.  
 
    Parameters: 
    - text (str): The text to be encrypted.  
Dahua-HTTP-API-For-DSS-V8.7_EN for pt_era_baru_digitama

--- PAGE 597 ---
 
596 
 
    - public_key_bytes (bytes): T he public key in bytes format.  
 
    Returns: 
    - bytes: The base64 encoded encrypted data.  
""" 
def encrypt_by_public_key(text, public_key_bytes):  
    public_key = RSA.import_key(public_key_bytes)  
    cipher = PKCS1_v1_5.new(public_key)  
    encrypted_data = cipher.encrypt(text.encode())  
    return base64.b64encode(encrypted_data)  
""" 
    Concatenates two byte sequences.  
     
    This function takes two byte sequences as input, checks if they are None, and if so, ass igns
 them an empty byte sequence.  
    Then it concatenates these two byte sequences and returns the result.  
     
    Parameters: 
    - bytes1: The first byte sequence, can be None.  
    - bytes2: The second byte sequence, can be None.  
     
    Returns: 
    - The concatenated byte sequence.  
""" 
def sum_bytes(bytes1, bytes2):  
    if bytes1 is None:  
        bytes1 = b''  
    if bytes2 is None:  
        bytes2 = b''  
    return bytes1 + bytes2  
 
def main():

de(platform_public_key_with_base64)) 
    encrypted_aes_secret_vector_with_base64 = encrypt_by_public_key(aes_secret_vector, base64. b64
decode(platform_public_key_with_base64))

6.3.2 MQ Connection Examples 
Get MQ Configuration 
Dahua-HTTP-API-For-DSS-V8.7_EN for pt_era_baru_digitama

--- PAGE 599 ---
 
598 
 
• MQ password is AES-encrypted. First, complete login authentication. The second 
login interface returns AES-decrypted secret key and vector. The secret key and 
vector have been encrypted with the RSA public key of the requester, and shall be 
decrypted by RSA private key of the requester. 
• See [3.2.1 Get MQ Configuration] to get server MQ configuration data. 
• Get the AES secret key and vector of the decrypted plain text. Use AES decryption 
method to decrypt the MQ password into plain text. 
• The client connects to the server through SSL. 
• When there may be different dependency packages listening to MQ, the naming 
format of the topic will be different, which is not our common "." sign separation. 
Take the alarm topic mq.alarm.msg.topic.{userId} as an example: 
Environment: Browser  
Dependent package:mqtt  
Protocol: ws/wss 
Topic format : mq/alarm/msg/topic/{userId} 
 
Environment: Node  
Dependent package: mqtt  
Protocol: mqtt/mqtts 
Topic format : mq/alarm/msg/topic/{userId} 
 
Environment: Node  
Dependent package:stompit  
Protocol: stomp 
Topic format : /topic/mq.alarm.msg.topic.{userId}

    /** 
     * Send post request method with HTTP.  
     * @param url URL string  
     * @param params interface params  
     * @return response data  
     */ 
    static String sendPost(String url, Map<String, Object> params) throws Exception {  
        if (params == null) {  
            params = new HashMap<>(0);  
        } 
        //Create a trust manager that does not validate certificate chains  
        TrustManager[] trustAllCerts = new TrustManager[] {  
            new X509TrustManager() {  
                @Override 
                public X509Certificate[] getAcceptedIssuers() {  
                    return new X509Certificate[0];  
                } 
                @Override 
                public void checkClientTrusted(X509Certificate[] certs, String authType) {  
                } 
                @Override 
                public void checkServerTrusted(X509Certificate[] certs, String authType) {  
                } 
            } 
        }; 
        //Install the all -trusting trust manager  
        try {  
            SSLContext sslContext = SSLContext.getInstance("SSL");  
            sslContext.init(null, trustAllCerts, new SecureRandom());  
            //Create an ssl socket factory with our all -trusting manager  
            SSLConnectionSocketFactory sslSocketFactory = new SSLConnectionSocketFactory(sslC
ontext, (hostname, session) -> true);  
 
            //Create a custom HttpClient with the SSL socket factory  
            CloseableHttpClient httpClient = HttpClients.custom()  
                    .setSSLSocketFactory(sslSocketFactory) 
                    .build(); 
            HttpEntityEnclosingRequestBase httpRequest = new HttpPost(url);;  
            StringEntity entity = new StringEntit y(JSON.toJSONString(params), "UTF -8"); 
            httpRequest.setEntity(entity); 
            httpRequest.setHeader("Content-Type", "application/json;charset=UTF -8"); 
            httpRequest.setHeader("X-Subject-Token", TOKEN_VALUE);  
 
            CloseableHttpResponse response = httpClient.execute(httpRequest);  
            HttpEntity responseEntity = response.getEntity();  
Dahua-HTTP-API-For-DSS-V8.7_EN for pt_era_baru_digitama

--- PAGE 603 ---
 
602 
 
            //In order to avoid messy code,encode the response data in UTF -8. 
            String reply = EntityUtils.toString(responseEntity, "UTF -8"); 
            //Release resources finally.  
            if (httpClient != null) {  
                httpClient.close(); 
            } 
            if (response != null) {  
                response.close(); 
            } 
            return reply;  
        } catch (NoSuchAlgorithmException | KeyManagementException e) {  
            throw new RuntimeException(e);  
        } 
    } 
 
    /** 
     * AES decryption, the mode is CBC, and the filling mod e is pkcs7padding  
     * @param text data  
     * @param aesKey AES key  
     * @param aesVector AES vector  
     * @return string after decryption  
     * @throws Exception  
     */ 
    static String decryptByAesCbc(String text, String aesKey, String aesVector ) throws Exception {  
        Security.addProvider(new BouncyCastleProvider());  
        byte[] raw = aesKey.getBytes(StandardCharsets.UTF_8);  
        SecretKeySpec skeySpec = new SecretKeySpec(raw, "AES");  
        Cipher cipher = Cipher.getInstance("AES/CBC /PKCS7Padding"); 
        IvParameterSpec iv = new IvParameterSpec(aesVector.getBytes(Stan dardCharsets.UTF_8)); 
        cipher.init(Cipher.DECRYPT_MODE, skeySpec, iv);  
        byte[] encrypted = parseHexStr2Byte(text);  
        byte[] originalPassByte = cipher.doFinal(encrypted);  
        return new String(originalPassByte, StandardCharsets.UTF_8);  
    } 
 
    /** 
     * Hex string to byte array  
     * @param hexStr hex str ing 
     * @return byte array  
     */ 
    static byte[] parseHexStr2Byte(String hexStr) {  
        byte[] result = new byte[hexStr.length() / 2];  
        for (int i = 0;i< hexStr.length() / 2; i++) {  
            int high = Integer.parseInt(hexStr.substring( i * 2, i * 2 + 1), 16);  
            int low = Integer.parseInt(hexStr.substring(i * 2 + 1, i * 2 + 2), 16);  
            result[i] = (byte) (high * 16 + low);  
        } 
        return result;  
    } 
 
    /** 
     * CustomerMqFactory, used by SSL connection  
     */ 
    static class CustomerMqFactory extends ActiveMQSslConnectionFactory {  
        @Override 
        protected TrustManager[] createTrustManager() {  
            return new TrustManager[]{

ket socket) {  
                    } 
                    @Override

cket socket) {  
                    } 
                    @Override 
                    public void checkClientTrusted(X509Certificate[] x509Certificates, String s,  SSL
Engine sslEngine) {  
                    } 
                    @Override

                    } 
                    @Override

                        return new X509Certificate[]{};  
                    } 
                } 
            }; 
        }

6.3.2.2 Example of MQ Connection with JS 
Description 
Use plug-ins to run utf8, hex, base64, AES, mqtt and import the plug-ins with ES6 or the 
<script> tag. 
// axios  
<script src="https://unpkg.com/axios/dist/axios.min.js"></script> 
// crypto -js 
<script type="text/javascript" src="path -to/bower_components/crypto-js/crypto-js.js"></script> 
// mqttjs  
<script src="https://cdn.bootcdn.net/ajax/libs/mqtt/4.2.8/mqtt.min.js"></script> 
For detailed instructions and description, go to the websites: 
axios.js - official document 
npm/crypto-js 
npm/mqtt

/** 
 * Send a POST request to  the specified URL with the given parameters.  
 * @param url  
 * @param params  
 * @returns {Promise<any>}  
 */ 
async function sendPost(url, params) {  
    if (params === null) {  
        params = {};  
    } 
 
    try {  
        const response = await axios.post(url, params, {  
            headers: {  
                'Content-Type': 'application/json;charset=UTF -8', 
                'X-Subject-Token': TOKEN_VALUE  
            }, 
            httpsAgent: new https.Agent({  
                rejectUnauthorized: false  
            }) 
        }); 
        //In order to avoid messy code, encode the response data in UTF -8. 
        return response.data;  
    } catch (error) {  
        throw error;  
    } 
} 
 
/** 
 * Listen to the MQ message.  
 * @param mqUrl  
 * @param userName  
 * @param userPassword  
 * @param messageName  
 * @param messageType  
 */ 
function listenMqMessage(mqUrl, userName, userPassword, messageName, me ssageType) {  
    console.log(mqUrl) 
    const client = mqtt.connect(mqUrl,{  
        clientId: 'client -1', 
        username: userName,  
        password: userPassword,  
        rejectUnauthorized: false,  
    }); 
    client.on('connect', function () {  
        const topicOrQueue = messageType ===  TOPIC ? messageName : messageName;  
        
        client.subscribe(topicOrQueue, (err, granted) => {  
            if (err) {  
              console.error('Subscription error:', err);  
            } else {  
              console.log('Subscribed to the topic successfully', granted);  
            } 
            }); 
Dahua-HTTP-API-For-DSS-V8.7_EN for pt_era_baru_digitama

--- PAGE 607 ---
 
606 
 
         
        }) 
    client.on('message', (topic, message) => {  
        console.log(`Received message on ${topic}: ${message.toString()}`);  
    }); 
    client.on('reconnect', () => {  
        console.log('Reconnecting to MQ');  
    }); 
 
    client.on('offline', () => {  
        console.log('Offline from MQ');  
    }); 
 
    client.on('close', () => {  
        console.log('Connection closed');  
    }); 
} 
 
/** 
 * AES encryption mode is CBC, and  the filling mode is pkcs7padding.  
 * @param text  
 * @param secretKey  
 * @param secretVector  
 * @returns {string}  
 */ 
function decryptByAesCbc(text, secretKey, secretVector) {  
    const key = utf8.parse(secretKey);  
    const iv = utf8.parse(secretVector);  
    const encryptedHexWord = hex.parse(text);  
    const srcs = base64.stringify(encryptedHexWord);  
    const decrypt = AES.decrypt(srcs, key, { iv });  
    const decryptedWord = decrypt.toString(utf8);  
    return decryptedWord.toString();  
} 
 
main();

        static String SendPost(String url, Dictionary<String, Object>? param)  
        {

            HttpRequestMessage httpRequestMessage = new(HttpMethod.Post, url);

        /** 
         * Sending ht tp requests asynchronously.  
         * @param httpRequestMessage  
         * @return response  
         */ 
        public static async Task<string> SendAsync(HttpRequestMessage httpRequest Message) 
        { 
           // Create a custom HttpClientHandler and  ignore certificate validation  
            HttpClientHandler handler = new HttpClientHandler  
            { 
                ServerCertificateCustomValidationCallback = (message, cert, chain, sslPolicyErr ors) 
=> true  
            }; 
            HttpClient httpClient = new HttpClient(handler);  
            HttpResponseMessage response = await httpClient.SendAsync(httpRequestMessa ge); 
 
            //In order to avoid messy code,encode the response data in UTF -8. 
            string reply = await response.Content.R eadAsStringAsync(); 
            return reply;  
        } 
 
        /** 
         * AES encryption mode is CBC, and the filling mode is pkcs7padding.  
         * @param text

         * @param aesKey  
         * @param aesVector

        public static String DecryptWithAES7(String? text, String aesKey, String aesVe ctor) 
        { 
          byte[] raw = Encoding.UTF8.GetBytes(aesKey);  
            using (Aes aesAlg = Aes.Cre ate()) 
            { 
                aesAlg.Key = raw;  
                aesAlg.IV = Encoding.UTF8.GetBytes(aesVector);  
                aesAlg.Mode = CipherMode.CBC;  
                aesAlg.Padding = PaddingMode.PKCS7;  
 
                ICryptoTransform decryp tor = aesAlg.CreateDecryptor(aesAlg.Key, aesAlg.IV);  
                byte[] encrypted = ParseHexStr2Byte(text);  
                byte[] originalPassByte = decryptor.TransformFinalBlock(encrypted, 0, en crypted.Le
ngth); 
                return Encoding.UTF8.Ge tString(originalPassByte); 
            } 
        } 
 
        /** 
         * Parse hex string to byte array.  
         *  
         * @param hexStr  
         * @return  
         */ 
        public static byte[] ParseHexStr2Byte(string hexStr)  
        { 
            byte[] result = new byte[hexStr.Length / 2];  
            for (int i = 0; i < hexStr.Length / 2; i++)  
            { 
                int high = Convert.ToInt32(hexStr.Substrin g(i * 2, 1), 16);  
                int low = Convert.ToInt32(hexStr.Substring(i * 2 + 1, 1), 16);  
                result[i] = (byte)(high * 16 + low);  
            } 
            return result;  
        }

    secret_key = "9c9d026........ae8a231a8d6"  
    secret_vector = "b6d3........91cc"  
    user_password = decrypt_by_aes_cbc(user_password_with_aes, secret_key, s ecret_vector) 
 
    # Step3: Initialize the MQ connection information, and start the message listening.  
    message_name = f"mq.event.msg.topic.{user_id}"  
    print(user_password) 
    listen_mq_message_stomp(mq_url_addr, user_name, user_password, message_name , TOPIC)

def send_post(url, params=None):

    print(headers) 
    response = requests.post(url, headers=headers, json=params, verify= False) 
    print(response.text) 
    response.raise_for_status() 
    return response.text  
 
""" 
    Connects to a Message Queue (MQ) using the STOMP protocol and listens for messages.  
 
    Parameters: 
    - mq_url (str): The URL of the MQ server in the format "host:port".  
    - user_name (str): The username for connecting to the MQ.  
    - password (s tr): The password for connecting to the MQ.  
    - message_name (str): The name of the topic or queue to subscribe to.  
    - message_type (str): The type of message destination, either 'topic' or 'que ue'. 
 
    Returns: 
    - None: If the `message_type` is neither 'topic' nor 'queue', the function returns immedi ately. 
     
    Summary: 
    This function establishes an SSL -enabled connection to the MQ server using STOMP. It subs
cribes to either a topic or a queue based on the `message_type` parameter and s tarts listening f
or incoming messages. A non -blocking loop prevents the program from exiting prematurely.  
""" 
def listen_mq_message_stomp(mq_url, user_name, password, message_name, mes sage_type): 
    if message_type not in [TOPIC, QUEUE]:  
        return 
 
    # Use Connection with SSL support  
    conn = stomp.Connection12(host_and_ports=[(mq_url.split(":")[0], int(mq_url.sp lit(":")[1]))]) 
    conn.set_listener('', PrintingListener())  
    # Configure SSL manually  
    ssl_params = {  
        'key_file': None,  
        'cert_file': None,  
        'ca_certs': None,  
        'ssl_version': ssl.PROTOCOL_TLSv1_2  
    } 
    conn.transport.set_ssl([(mq_url.split(":")[0], int(mq_url.split(":")[1]))], **ssl_param s) 
    conn.connect(user_name, password, wait=True)  
    if message_type == TOPIC:  
        conn.subscribe(destination=f"/topic/{message_name}", id=1, ack='auto')  
Dahua-HTTP-API-For-DSS-V8.7_EN for pt_era_baru_digitama

    else: 
        conn.subscribe(destination=f"/queue/{message_name}", id=1, ack='auto')  
 
    print("Start listening...")  
 
    # Th e method of listening to MQ is non blocking, while loop prevents program exit  
    while True:  
        time.sleep(10) 
 
""" 
    Decrypts the given text using AES -CBC mode.  
 
    :param text: The encrypted text, which should be a hexadecimal encoded string.  
    :param aes_key: The AES key used for decryption.  
    :param aes_vector: The initialization vector (IV) used for decryption.  
    :return: The decrypted text as a UTF -8 string.  
""" 
def decrypt_by_aes_cbc(text, aes_key, aes_vector):  
    key = bytes(aes_key, 'utf -8') 
    iv = bytes(aes_vector, 'utf -8') 
    cipher = AES.new(key, AES.MODE_CBC, iv)  
    encrypted = unhexlify(text)  
    decrypted = unpad(cipher.decrypt(encrypted), AES.block_size)  
    return decrypted.decode('utf -8')

    main() 
6.4 Encryption and Decryption Example 
The VMS platform uses encryption algorithms such as MD5, RSA, and AES for encryption 
and decryption. The development language used in the example is JAVA, which has been 
verified in JDK1.8.0_381. The client and platform interact with each other, involving 
encryption and decryption fields, using the AES algorithm. The RSA algorithm is only used 
to encrypt AES key and vector, and is not used for encryption of other business fields. 
MD5 Encryption 
String text = "0123456789ABCDEF";  
//Encryption 
String encryptTextByMd5 = encryptByMd5(text);  
 
/** 
* MD5 encryption  
* @param text data  
* @return string after encryption  
* @throws Exception  
*/ 
public static String encryptByMd5(String text) throws Exception {  
    MessageDigest md = MessageDigest.getInstance("MD5");  
    byte[] messageDigest = md.digest(text.getBytes());  
    StringBuilder buffer = new StringBuilder();  
    for (byte b : messageDigest) {  
    buffer.append(String.format("%02x", b));

    } 
    return buffer.toString();  
} 
RSA Encryption and Decryption 
String text = "0123456789ABCDEF";  
//Generate key pairs

PrivateKey privateKey = keyPair.getPrivate();

/** 
* Generate RSA public key and private key. The private key is in pkcs8 format, an d the public k
ey is in X509 forma t 
* @return key pair  
* @throws Exception  
*/ 
public static KeyPair getRsaKeys() throws Exception {  
    Provider provider = Security.getProvider("SunRsaSign");  
    KeyPairGenerator keyPairGen = KeyPairGenerator.getInstance("RSA", provide r); 
    keyPairGen.initialize(2048, new SecureRandom());  
    KeyPair keyPair = keyPairGen.generateKeyPair();  
    return keyPair;  
} 
 
/** 
 * RSA encryption. Public key encryption, p rivate key decryption  
 * @param text data  
 * @param publicKeyBytes public key string array  
 * @return string after encryption  
 * @throws Exception  
 */ 
public static byte[] encryptByPublicKey(String text, byte[] publicKeyBytes) th rows Exception {  
    byte[] result = null;  
    int rsaBytesLenEncrypt = 245;  
 
    //Get public key object  
    X509EncodedKeySpec x509KeySpec = new X509EncodedKeySpec(publicKeyBytes);  
    KeyFactory keyFactory = KeyFactory.getInstance("RSA");  
    Key publicKeyObject = keyFactory.gene ratePublic(x509KeySpec); 
 
    //Encrypt data  
    byte[] dataBytes = text.getBytes(StandardCharsets.UTF_8);  
    Cipher cipher = Cipher.getInstance(keyFactory.getAlgorithm());  
    cipher.init(Cipher.ENCRYPT_MODE, publicKeyObject);  
    for (int i = 0; i < dataBytes.length; i += rsaBytesLenEncrypt) {  
        int to = Math.min(i + rsaBytesLenEncrypt, dataBytes.length);  
        byte[] temp = cipher.doFinal(Arrays.copyOfRange(dataBytes, i, to));  
        result = sumBytes(result, temp);  
Dahua-HTTP-API-For-DSS-V8.7_EN for pt_era_baru_digitama

615 
 
    } 
    return result;  
} 
 
/** 
 * RSA decryption. Public key encryption, private key decryption  
 * @param text data  
 * @param privateKeyBytes private key string array  
 * @return string after decryption  
 * @throws Exception  
 */ 
public static byte[] decryptByPrivateKey(String text, byte[] privateKey Bytes) throws Exception {  
    byte[] result = null;  
    int rsaBytesLenDecrypt = 256;  
    byte[] dataBytes = parseHexStr2Byte(text);  
 
    //Get private key obj ect 
    PKCS8EncodedKeySpec pkcs8KeySpec = new PKCS8EncodedKeySpec(privateKe yBytes); 
    KeyFactory keyFactory = KeyFactory.getInstance("RSA");  
    Key privateKey = keyFactory.generatePrivate(pkcs8KeySpec);  
 
    //Decrypt data  
    Cipher cipher = Cipher.getInstance(keyFactory.getAlgorithm());  
    cipher.init(Cipher.DECRYPT_MODE, privateKey);  
 
    for (int i = 0; i < dataBytes.length; i += rsaBytes LenDecrypt) {  
        int to = (i + rsaBytesLenDecrypt) < dataBytes.length ? (i + rsaBytesLenDecry pt) : dataBy
tes.length; 
        byte[] temp = cipher.doFinal(Arrays.copyOfRange(dataBytes, i, to));  
        result = sumBytes(result, temp);  
    } 
 
    return result; 
} 
 
/** 
 * Hex string to byte array  
 * @param hexStr hex string  
 * @return byte array  
 */ 
private static byte[] parseHexStr2Byte(String hexStr) {  
    byte[] result = new byte[hexStr.length() / 2];  
    for (int i = 0; i < hexStr.length() / 2; i++) {  
        int high = Integer.parseInt(hexStr.substring(i * 2, i * 2 + 1), 16);  
        int low = Integer.parseInt(hexStr.substring(i * 2 + 1, i * 2 + 2), 16);  
        result[i] = (byte) (high * 16 + low);  
    } 
    return result;  
} 
 
/** 
 * Sum 2 bytes  
 * @param bytes1 byte 1  
 * @param bytes2 byte 2  
 * @return the new array formed by merging two arrays  
 */ 
private static byte[] sumBytes(byte[] bytes1, byte[] bytes2) {  
Dahua-HTTP-API-For-DSS-V8.7_EN for pt_era_baru_digitama

--- PAGE 617 ---
 
616 
 
    byte[] result = null;  
    int len1 = 0;  
    int len2 = 0;  
    if (null != bytes1) {  
        len1 = bytes1.length;  
    } 
    if (null != bytes2) {  
        len2 = bytes2.length;  
    } 
    if (len1 + len2 > 0) {  
        result = new byte[len1 + len2];  
    } 
    if (len1 > 0) {  
        System.arraycopy(bytes1, 0, result, 0, le n1); 
    } 
    if (len2 > 0) {  
        System.arraycopy(bytes2, 0, result, len1, len2);  
    } 
    return result;  
} 
AES Encryption and Decryption 
String text = "0123456789ABCDEF";  
//Generate key and vector

//Encryption

//Decryption 
String decryptTextByAesCbc = dec ryptByAesCbc(encryptTextByAesCbc, aesKey, aesVector);  
 
/** 
 * AES encryption, the mode is CBC, and the filling mode is pkcs7padding  
 * If you cannot provide BouncyCastleProvider(), you can comment out this code "Security.addP ro
vider(new BouncyCastleProvider())", and change "AES/CCB/PKCS7Padding" to "AES/C CB/PKCS5Paddi
ng" in the following code  
 * @param text data  
 * @param aesKey AES ke y 
 * @param aesVector AES vector  
 * @return string after encryption  
 * @throws Exception  
 */ 
public static String encryptByAesCbc(String text, String aesKey, String aesV ector) throws Exception 
{ 
    //If you cannot provide BouncyCastleProvider(), you can comment out this code and change 
"AES/CCB/PKCS7Padding" to "AES/CCB/PKCS5Padding" in the following code.  
    Security.addProvider(new BouncyCastleProvider());  
    byte[] raw = aesKey.getBytes(StandardCharsets.UTF_8);  
    SecretKeySpec skeySpec = new SecretKeySpec(raw, "AES");  
    Cipher cipher = Cipher.getInstance("AES/CBC/PKCS7Padding");  
    IvParameterSpec iv = new IvParameterSpec(aesVector.getBytes(StandardC harsets.UTF_8)); 
    cipher.init(Cipher.ENCRYPT_MODE, skeySpec, iv);  
    byte[] encrypted = cipher. doFinal(text.getBytes(StandardCharsets.UTF_8)); 
    return parseByte2HexStr(encrypted).toLowerCase();  
}

/** 
 * AES decryption, the mode is CBC, and the filling mode is pkcs7padding  
 * If you cannot provide BouncyCastleProvider(), you can comment out this code "Security.addPro
vider(new BouncyCastleProvider())", and change "AES/CCB/PKCS7Padding" to "AES/C CB/PKCS5Paddi
ng" in the following code  
 * @param text data  
 * @param aesKey AES key  
 * @param aesVector AES vector  
 * @return string after decryption  
 * @th rows Exception  
 */ 
public static String decryptByAesCbc(String text, String aesKey, String aes Vector) throws Exception 
{ 
    Security.addProvider(new BouncyCastleProvider());  
    byte[] raw = aesKey.getBytes(StandardCharsets.UTF_8);  
    SecretKeySpec skeySpec = new SecretKeySpec(raw, "AES");  
    Cipher cipher = Cipher.getInstance("AES/CBC/PKCS7Padding");  
    IvParameterSpec iv = new IvParameterSpec(aesVector.getBytes(StandardC harsets.UTF_8)); 
    cipher.init(Cipher.DECRYPT_MODE, skeySpec, iv);  
    byte[] encrypted = parseHexStr2Byte(text);  
    byte[] originalPassByte = cipher.doFinal(encrypted);  
    return new String(originalPassByte, StandardCharsets.UTF_8);  
} 
 
/** 
 * Byte arra y to hex string  
 * @param bytes byte array  
 * @return hex string  
 */ 
private static String parseByte2HexStr(byte[] bytes) {  
    StringBuffer buffer = new StringBuffer();  
    for (int i = 0; i < bytes.length; i++) {  
        String hex = Integer.toHexString( bytes[i] & 0xFF);  
        if (hex.length() == 1) {  
            hex = '0' + hex;  
        } 
        buffer.append(hex); 
    } 
    return buffer.toString();  
} 
 
/** 
 * Hex string to byte array  
 * @param hexStr hex string  
 * @return byte array  
 */ 
private static byte[] parseHexStr2Byte(String hexStr) {  
    byte[] result = new byte[hexStr.length() / 2];  
    for (int i = 0; i < hexStr.length() / 2; i++) {  
        int high = Integer.parseInt(hexStr.substring(i * 2, i * 2 + 1),  16); 
        int low = Integer.parseInt(hexStr.substring(i * 2 + 1, i * 2 + 2), 16);  
        result[i] = (byte) (high * 16 + low);  
    } 
    return result;  
}

7 FAQ 
7.1 Common Errors 
7.1.1 Image URL cannot be opened 
Q: The interface return value or MQ message includes an image URL as follows. 
https://192.168.1.1:50001/afefb58d-5b66-11e9-8037-000000000000/20190612/1/dsf_739dc016-8d79-
11e9-9f8a-000000000000_34782193_34998401.jpg 
After copying the URL to the browser bar, the image cannot be opened. 
A: To get image resources, you need to add the authentication token as follows. 
https://192.168.1.1:50001/afefb58d-5b66-11e9-8037-000000000000/20190612/1/dsf_739dc016-8d79-
11e9-9f8a-000000000000_34782193_34998401.jpg?token=122dc1ecda074d1ea6b5e8865ef028bb 
This token is different from the token sent in the interface request header X-Subject-
Token. Instead, it comes from the return value credential of the [3.1.2 Submit Credentials] 
interface, but also follows the same expiration mechanism: Without heartbeat keep-alive, 
the credential expires after 30 seconds. With heartbeat keep-alive, the credential expires 
after 30 minutes. So you must add a valid credential to the end of the image URL.  
If the image still cannot be opened, open it on the VMS client. If the image cannot be 
opened on the VMS client, the image might not have been stored for the lack of image 
disk. If the image can be opened on the VMS client, the token might have been expired. 
Another case is that the image URL includes "?" as follows: 
https://192.168.1.1:8082/1000054$1$0$0/20210206/23/5457-3196639-0.jpg?streamID:1260@capTime:
1612684797 
In this case, you must use "&" to add the token. 
https://192.168.1.1:8082/1000054$1$0$0/20210206/23/5457-3196639-0.jpg?streamID:1260@capTime:
1612684797&token=122dc1ecda074d1ea6b5e8865ef028bb 
7.1.2 RTSP URL cannot pull stream 
Q: While playing videos on VLC after getting the live video RTSP URL from the interface, 
users still need to enter the username and password or the platform reports error. 
Dahua-HTTP-API-For-DSS-V8.7_EN for pt_era_baru_digitama

--- PAGE 621 ---
 
620 
 
A: We recommend you call [3.4.1 Start Real-time Video] to get the live video RTSP URL, 
and then pull stream with standard decoding tools (such as VLC) or DPSDK.  
Return data of the interface: 
{ 
    "data": {  
        "minRate": null,  
        "protocol": null,  
        "ip": null,  
        "port": null,  
        "stunEnable": null,  
        "stunPort": null,  
        "url": "rtsp://192.168.1.1:9100/vms/monitor/param/cameraid=1000040%240%26substream=1
", 
        "url2": "",  
        "connectType": null,  
        "session": "2204",  
        "token": "2204",  
        "trackId": ""  
    } 
} 
When requesting a video, use the token field as a URL parameter. Otherwise, the video 
request will fail. 
This token is different from the token in X-Subject-Token and is returned by MTS. Each 
token expires after being used once, or not used within 30 seconds. The token for 
continuous stream pulling does not need to be updated.  
The format of an URL with token is as follows: 
rtsp://192.168.1.1:9100/vms/monitor/param/cameraid=1000040%240%26substream=1?
token=2204 
In addition, there is another situation where in the internal and external network 
environment, the platform may return multiple streaming addresses, separated by "|", 
namely the intranet address and the external network address. When using it, you need 
to separate it into multiple addresses according to the network environment of the 
current login platform, and finally splice the token at the end. For example, the address 
returned by the platform is: 
rtsp://192.168.1.1:9100/vms/monitor/param/cameraid=1000040%240%26substream=1|r
tsp://10.10.10.10:9100/vms/monitor/param/cameraid=1000040%240%26substream=1 
Among them, 192.168.1.1 is the intranet IP, and 10.10.10.10 is the external IP. If you are 
currently docking in an external network environment, the final streaming address is 
rtsp://10.10.10.10:9100/vms/monitor/param/cameraid=1000040%240%26substream=1?
token=2204

7.1.3 Failed to get real-time alarms after listening to MQ 
Q: After listening to a MQ alarm topic, users cannot receive alarms. 
A: Multiple reasons might cause the problem. 
1 Failed to configure linked users. For users to receive alarms from the platform, you 
must configure linked users while configuring the alarm protocols. Check whether the 
VMS client can receive real-time alarms. If yes, configurations are normal. If no, contact 
the technical support. 
2 Listening to wrong MQ alarm topics. To receive alarms, you need to listen to 
mq.alarm.msg.topic.{userId}. UserID is the ID of the login user, it can be obtained through 
the [3.1.2 Submit Credentials] interface. For example, if the userID of the login user is 100, 
listen to mq.alarm.msg.topic.100. 
3 Users are offline. Alarms, events and other messages on the platform are only sent to 
online users by default (System users are excluded). After logging in to the platform 
through the API, you need to call [3.1.3 Heartbeat Keep-alive] and [3.1.4 Update Token] 
interfaces to keep online status. Otherwise, alarm messages will not be sent to the related 
MQ topics. During test, keep the user online on the VMS client to check whether the user 
can receive alarm messages. After the test, keep the user online through API interface. 
7.1.4 No image information in the alarm messages 
Q: No image information is included in the alarm messages. 
A: Listen to mq.alarm.msg.topic.{userId} to get alarm events. See [4.2.1 Alarm Messages]. 
Only few intelligent alarms support automatic capture. Get the snapshots with 
alarmPicture. Snapshots of other linked cameras are reported asynchronously. Listen to 
mq.event.msg.topic.{userId} to link snapshots. See [4.2.3 Notification of Alarm Images]. 
Alarm messages and images are interconnected through alarmCode. 
7.1.5 No person information in the alarm messages 
Q: No person information is included in the access control alarm messages. 
A: Listen to mq.alarm.msg.topic.{userId} to get alarm events. See [4.2.1 Alarm Messages]. 
The messages only include the basic information about an event. For linked information 
such as persons, faces, entrances and exits and traffic, call other interfaces. For example, 
to obtain personnel information of access control alarms, refer to [3.6.10 Get Alarm 
Related Access Control Information] and associate through the alarmCode field. 
Dahua-HTTP-API-For-DSS-V8.7_EN for pt_era_baru_digitama
